×

所謂凡人就是聞譽由沾沾自喜，聞毀則悶悶不悅。

×

所謂凡人就是：有許多許多不好的事，他都是明知而故犯。

也談抄襲 179

— 文宗孔

文人抄襲，古時早有發現，不過大都屬於詩家，他們偶然在前人的詩詞中，擷取一二佳句，藉使自己的作品，可以生色，目的是盜些聲名而已，倒並無利的念頭。像何遜詩「薄雲　際出，初月渡中上」杜甫換去四個字，「薄雲嚴際宿，孤月浪中翻。」便成為杜詩了。又像林　把江為詩「竹影橫斜水清淺，桂香浮動月黃昏。」換「竹」為「疎」，易「桂」作「暗」，也就變成他的詠梅詩了。

但是到了今日，抄襲之風，蔚然昌盛，且有公開與走私之分，前者像市上所出版的「文摘」刊物，他們不外有兩種宗旨；（一）因為大好文章，讀者不容易全部看到，所以他們就實行博搜選摘，蒐集著刊載起來，以便讀者的閱覽便利。（二）因為這樣一來，對於他們稿費的支出，未嘗不可以節省。

往往有一般墮落的文人，為了生活的威協，感覺一般報紙和雜志，又難於使自已不夠水準的文章，被編者錄取刊登，於是不得不冒著危險，動了卑劣的腦筯。翻翻數年前他處已經刊載的較好文章，或是一些偏僻雜誌上的幽默翻譯，將它改頭換面一下，抄好了向報館裏一送，這樣的稿件，自然容易發表，那末他也就可以靜候稿費了。

但是處於園丁地位的編者，雖然對於自已的園地十分珍視，不過單憑著他僅有的一些限力與時間，決不易縝密地辦別各處農場寄來繁雜的種籽，因此待到遊客的光臨，才會給他們指摘出。這是不值栽培的　草，那是已經變種的花兒！

本月十日自由談的園地裏，居然被一位懷伊子先生，也在遊園的時候，發現了八月一日所載署名為「淩捉煙」投稿的「聰明與傻瓜」一文，竟是抄襲三十三年六月十二日出版之「潮流」叢刊第一二四頁丹心先生所作之「聰明人與傻瓜」。我覺得此公非常膽大，不過有趣的是被揭發的文章，卻恰巧題目為「聰明與傻瓜」，是不是文曲星在冥冥之中玩弄文抄公，說他聰明人反變為傻瓜呢？

看了「編輯室」的揭發抄襲所載，那位抄襲者也夠慘了，在這樣的情形下，我們還要「罔談彼短」的戳壁腳，似乎有傷忠厚，但是顧念到這塊珍貴的寸金之地，為保護嘉禾的滋長，與體恤園丁的精力，我們遊園的一群，就不能不咬緊牙根，放出尖銳的眼光，協助編者，來拔除那魚目混珠的稗草，使將來能得到優良的收獲！

時事雜感

羊毛出在誰身上 180

— 范正邦

吳市長說兩年後收買跑馬廳羊毛出在身上，似乎即以跑馬廳收來之款收買跑馬廳，合算之至。其實出羊毛的羊是誰，不是十九為中國百姓嗎？外國人允許送給市府的羊毛不是出在中國羊的身上嗎，而同時外國人卻收去了更多的羊毛。此語自外國人　來方為確當，吳市長的算盤反被外國商人打了去哩。我們旁觀者清，此乃吳市長之政聲之關鍵，如果我是吳市長的智囊，我要勸吳市長隨參議會去議決，乃屬上策。如果加以說項，斯為下策。若能加以反對，斯乃最上上策。若雲兩年後收買誰又能擔保？去年底前五千元法幣可買一擔上好白米，此刻買不到一鬥好米。要買不如現在集合投資或中外合辦有利事業，於此偌大基地上。我想爽脆回絕於其既跑而拿其錢之後再禁其不跑耶？

兩點意見：第一，羊毛出在誰身上？第二，兩年之後的事，誰能保證？親愛的市長，尊從人民的意見吧！人民會擁戴你的！

校長的如意算盤 181

— 菖蒲

日昨友人張君來訪，因為二人都是教育界中人，所以話題不離本行，隨後談到教員的進退問題上去。他告訴我一椿令人發指的事情，使我不得不把它記錄下來。讓讀者知道世界上還有這種令人啼笑皆非的事。

事情是這樣的：八月廿五日張君看到報載滬東某小學擬聘請男女教員數位的啟事，他就將履歷寄去，二天之後接到一信，叫他在廿九日上午赴大西路某某小學面洽試教事宜，他以為事情必是稍有希望了，豈知該日上午親往該校時，原來是一個簡陋的衛堂小學，僅僅六七十個學生，校長兼打鐘的校役，學生抬風琴，泡開水，兼做雜差。那位校長先生神氣十足，擺出似理不理的態度，當時使張君已經起了孤疑，後來叫他當日擔任了好幾個鐘點的課程，沒有水喝，弄得精疲力盡，口幹舌燥，才讓他回去，臨時說過不論聘請與否，隔日必給他回信，可是張君回家後等了五六天，竟毫音訊。知道已經上了當，自已費了事資，又在大熱天替他教書，「賠了夫人又折兵」了。原來那個精明的校長恐怕開學遲了學生會拉不住，所以提早開課；但又不願老教員自八月起薪，所以想出這種法子來。說得好聽些是請新教員試教，實際上卻是替他自已省去八月份薪津的支出。

凡此種種，真令人無話可說。

新聞人物

閩臺清查團長劉文島　臺灣打虎去 182

— 君默

閩臺接收工作清查團團長劉文島到了臺灣，十二日招待記者，說：「我們此次來臺，是要打老虎，不是拍蒼蠅。」

見過劉文島的人，都可以相信他是能打幾下老虎的：高高的身材，結實的個子，方頭大耳，雖然似乎常常掛著張笑葉嘻嘻的臉孔，但不大說話，使人難以猜出他會要想做點什麼？

軍人出身

這是一位軍人出身的政治家，他半生的事業，一半化在自已的故鄉湖北，劉文島和漢口市的關係是特別悠長；另一半則化在國外—德國和意大利。他在保定軍校畢業以後，也和許多同班同學們一樣，到了日本，但他對於帶兵似乎一直是興趣很少，所以不久便去了法國，在巴黎大學學法律。回國的時候，正值北伐的大業展開；他，一個學過軍事而後轉到了法律路上的三十四幾的年青人，便擔任了國民革命軍前敵總指揮部的政治部主任。北伐軍占領了漢口，他便出任了這南北樞紐之城的市長。那時候，久被軍閥盤據的漢口，一切都還是亂糟糟，尤其又因為漢口的有特區和法日租界，治理上更多困難，就以交通這件事來說，那時漢口的人力車不能拉進特區和租界，特區和租界的人力車也不能夠拉出來。這件事情使交通上發生極多困難，經過了劉氏多次和租界當局的交涉，才算兩邊的「通軍」成功。但想不到這一段小小的「國際交涉」，卻正是他以後一長段的外交事業的開始。

一度使德

二十年，劉氏出任駐德公使；以後，又轉任駐義大利公使。戰前的幾年，中國和義大利間的關係，相當良好，尤其是航空方面，在飛機及飛行的訓練上，合作很多，當時杭州　橋的中央航空學校，大部分的外籍教官都是義大處人。劉氏在航空合作方面所作的工作，貢獻很大。但是二十六年，八一三戰起，這批忘恩負義的義大利教官卻坐在日本轟炸機裏，把杭州的火軍站炸成了個空殼，這又豈是劉氏當初所能料及呢！

頗懂幽默

劉文島頗有點幽默，但不大肯留情面。在他做漢口市長的時候，那裏有一位鼎鼎大名的堪與大家，名叫做丁壽陽，在漢口也混了有二十多年了。專替人看墳地風水，據說是無不中，市政府裏有一位局長對他信服得了不得，介紹了他到市長公館去，物色一棺佳城的牛眠吉地。這位風水先生在劉文島前面吹得個天花亂墜，說是看了這麼一塊墳地，必可以榮華富貴，萬世其昌。劉一聲不響，等他說完了，過了好半天，才慢吞吞地問道：「既然是這樣，那你可不先替自已看一塊呢？」把這位澆了一頭冷水的堪與大家，趕出了大門。

這自然只是拍了一只蒼蠅，但劉氏這次是自已去看看臺灣的風水了，想必可以扳一扳同樣的冷面孔，打它幾頭老虎回來吧！

連環漫畫　三毛從軍記（一○二） 183

— 張樂平作

上海橫斷面之三 184

學校兒童沿街零食、可當心病從口入

— 季清攝

1946.09.17

Important Consultations Held in Beiping; Chen Cheng and Du Yuming Arrive in Shenyang; Communist Army to Launch Offensive in Liaoning Province 1

Chen Cheng, Du Yuming

[Report from our Beiping office, 16th] Chen Cheng and Du Yuming flew to Shenyang from Beiping at 2:00 PM today. It is reported that Chen's visit to the north was to discuss with Li Zongren and others matters such as military reorganization, defense deployment, and is also said to be related to the restoration of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway traffic. Last night, Chen invited Li Zongren, Sun Lianzhong, Chen Jicheng, Wang Hongshao (Chief of Staff of the Provisional Headquarters), Song Yuntang, and Li Wen, Chief of Intelligence of the Commander-in-Chief's Office, to a military meeting, which lasted until after 1:00 AM. After 9:00 AM this morning, more than 30 leading figures from the party, government, and military of Beiping and Tianjin, including Li Zongren, Sun Lianzhong, Chen Jicheng, Xiong Bin, Zhang Boying, Mou Tingfang, and Hu Bohan, visited Chen at the Diplomatic Building. Du Yuming also accompanied them, bringing many others. In the spacious living room, they conducted a broad and informal review of various issues in North China. In addition, Chen had separate talks with Feng Qinzai, Chairman of Chahar Province, Zheng Jiemin, member of the Executive Headquarters, and Xu Kangliang, Commander of the Beiping Air Force District. Chen took a trip to the Summer Palace yesterday amidst his busy schedule and also visited Hu Shi and Fu Sinian. It is reported that Chen flew from Gu to Zheng on the 8th and inspected the areas around Kaifeng, Lanfeng, and Xinxiang. He only flew to Beiping yesterday with Du Yuming and Gao Guizi.

[Report from our Beiping office, 16th] Du Yuming accompanied Chen Cheng to Shenyang by plane today. Before his departure, he told our reporter that there would not be large-scale military conflicts in the Northeast recently, but if the Communist army attacked, the National army would resolutely counterattack at any time. This trip to Gu was to report the situation in the Northeast to the Chairman. When the reporter asked what instructions the Chairman had for the Northeast, Du replied that the Chairman instructed the Northeast to pay attention to restoring order and stabilizing people's livelihood. Du's face was much fuller than when he was recuperating in Beiping. He left Gu and flew to Zhengzhou on the 14th and arrived in Beiping yesterday on the same plane as Chen Cheng.

[Report from our Beiping office, 16th] If the Communist army does not lift the siege of Datong, will the National army attack Zhangjiakou? Chief of Staff Chen Cheng answered this question very cleverly. He said: "You can study and research it. If the Communist army does not lift the siege, is it better for the government forces to clear the Tongpu Road or attack Zhangjiakou?" The reporter pressed: "Didn't the Chief of Staff once say that Datong and Zhangjiakou are on the same battlefield?" Chen replied: "I said it, but it's a common practice in military strategy to make the real seem unreal and the unreal seem real." When asked about his mission to the Northeast, he cautiously said that he had not yet decided to go. Three hours later, he and General Du Yuming flew to Shenyang. Today, reporters from this newspaper and Ta Kung Pao only had a three-minute conversation with General Chen. It was when he was walking and talking as he got out of the building and into the car. Chen looked rosy, and his stomach ailment seemed to have healed, but his hair was even whiter than silver.

[Report from our Shenyang office, 16th] Chief of Staff Chen Cheng, accompanied by Chief Du Yuming, arrived at Beiling Airport at 4:30 PM on the 16th. Director Xiong and others went to welcome him. Those who came with Chief of Staff Chen included Xu Langxuan, Chief of the First Division of the Third Bureau of the Ministry of National Defense, and Gao Dechang, Chief of the Third Section of the same division. Chen told our reporter: "This is my first time in the Northeast. After arriving in Shenyang, I saw that many places in Shenyang were destroyed, but Shenyang is still our Shenyang. Everyone should work hard to build this land. This trip is to see the situation in the Northeast. I haven't decided where to go from here yet." Chen looked energetic and very happy. Chief Du flew to Gu on the 12th and returned on the 16th. According to what he told the reporter: "This time, I went to see the Chairman to report on the recovery of Chengde and the suffering of the people. The Chairman is very concerned about the Northeast, especially hoping to restore order and stabilize people's livelihood." He accompanied Chief of Staff Chen to Zhengzhou on the 14th for inspection.

[Agence France-Presse, Beiping, 16th] According to sources from the Communist side, the Northeast government forces divided into three routes yesterday and began to attack Harbin. The battle is currently taking place near Taolaizhao on the north bank of the Songhua River. Du Yuming, Commander of the Northeast Security, has returned to his defense post after seeking instructions from Chairman Chiang in Lushan. Du will directly command the military operations to attack Harbin.

[Central News Agency, Shenyang, 15th] According to reports: the 33rd Regiment of the 11th Brigade of the Communist army and the 3rd Regiment of the Independent Division, attached with two mountain guns and rapid-fire guns each, launched a fierce attack on the National army stationed at Xin Kai Ling, ten kilometers southeast of Dashiqiao, at 5:00 PM on the 13th. As of 8:00 AM on the 14th, the battle was still ongoing. Based on the overall situation in recent days, it seems that the Communist army will launch a large-scale offensive in the north and south of Liaoning Province.

Communist Forces in Jining Completely Eliminated; National Army Vanguard Reaches Sumu; Datong Garrison Launches Attack to Recover Strongholds 2

[Central News Agency, Taiyuan, 16th] Starting on the morning of the 16th, the Datong National army launched attacks in multiple directions. As of 11:00 AM, they had recovered eight strongholds, including the Police Academy west of the city, Wulidian, Majunying, Zhujiazhuang, and the airport south of the city, Shuiquanwan, Beiyue Temple, and Zhoujiadian. On the east side of the city, the National army had crossed the Yu River and were advancing towards Qijiadian, Caifulou, and Shaling.

[Central News Agency, Taiyuan, 16th] More than 600 Communist troops in the Qilicun, Beiyue Temple, and Zhoujiadian areas south of Datong launched another attack on Nanguan and Wayao Lin around 10:00 PM on the 14th. After fierce fighting, they were repelled in the afternoon and are currently confronting the National army at a distance of 100 meters. On the same day, a unit of the Communist army, fifty kilometers south of Wulidian west of the city, infiltrated under the cover of mountain guns, but were suppressed by artillery fire from the city wall and fled back after suffering losses.

[Central News Agency, Gui Sui, 15th] The National army rescuing Datong continued to advance after recovering Jining. The vanguard has reached Sumu (one station away from Jining). There are currently no traces of the Communist army within thirty miles around Jining.

[Central News Agency, Taiyuan, 16th] The people in the two counties of Hequ and Pianguan in northwestern Shanxi suffered unspeakable hardships under the occupation of the Communist army. Wei Zhuwuying, fearing the people of Hequ County, led the security team to recover Pianguan City on the 12th, dividing his troops to capture Guanhekou in the north and Louziying in the south. On the 13th, they continued to capture Hequ County, and are now advancing towards the Xunzheng area. The people of the two counties are overjoyed to see the light of day again.

[Report from our Beiping office, 16th] Yesterday's air force reconnaissance report stated that there were no traces of the Communist army within fifty li around Jining. The Communist army in Jining adopted a centrifugal strategy, retreating in all directions. One branch retreating towards the northeast was bombed by the air force en route, suffering half casualties. It is reported that the Communist army suffered more than 20,000 casualties in the Jining campaign, most of whom were killed after arriving at the periphery to reinforce Jining. The coordination between the National army's land and air forces was extremely thorough.

[Report from our Gui Sui office, 15th] The National army cavalry yesterday pursued and attacked the defeated Communist forces of E Yousan and Liu Chunfang, which had fled from Jining. At Honghaizi, forty li east of the city, they annihilated most of the 358th Brigade, killing 400, capturing 200 alive, and seizing 900 rifles, 20 light and heavy machine guns, and several mountain guns. The Communist army was surrounded by the cavalry. Many had blood coming from their mouths and noses, and they kowtowed to beg for mercy. Also, merchants from Beiping to Sui said that they saw the National army of the 11th War Area arrive in Xiahuayuan when they passed through, and they were advancing westward towards Zhangyuan.

[Central News Agency, Gui Sui, 16th] The eastern section of the Ping Sui Railway is being actively repaired. In addition to the fact that passenger trains have already resumed service from Gui Sui to Fusheng Zhuang, because the Communist army was defeated in both the Zhuozishan and Jining campaigns and did not have time to damage the tracks, repairs are relatively easy. It is estimated that the railway will be open to traffic in about five more days. However, the water towers and bridges that were originally damaged are difficult to repair due to the huge engineering work involved. Only temporary pontoon bridges are being built, and water tankers are carried with the trains to supply water along the way.

National Army in Eastern Hebei Recovers Pinggu 3

[Report from our Beiping office, 16th] A general who came to Beiping from Tianjin this morning said that the National army has recovered Pinggu, the last county town in eastern Hebei occupied by the Communist army. The National army is currently conducting cautious mopping-up operations in the eastern Hebei plains covered by the green gauze curtains.

[Report from our Tianjin office, 16th] In the battles around Baoding, the Communist army is driving innocent civilians as the vanguard. For days, the Communist army has been attacking the National army at night, all driving civilians to form the vanguard, each holding hand grenades to charge and kill. After inspecting the corpses outside the trenches on the 15th and discovering the above situation, the National army has decided to use infiltration tactics to disintegrate the Communist army from behind in order to reduce the death rate in the war.

National Army Going North Points Directly at Huai'an and Huaibei; Communist Forces in Northern Jiangsu Show Signs of Wavering; Moving Towards Huai'an and Bao'ying to Save the Critical Situation 4

[Report from our Taixian office, 16th] In the northern battlefront of northern Jiangsu, due to the National army pointing directly at Huai'an and Huaibei, the Communist army has shown signs of wavering. The Communist forces in the areas of Dongtai, Xinghua, and Yancheng are moving towards the area between Huai'an and Bao'ying in an attempt to save the critical situation. The Communist army in Shaobo is stepping up its defenses in view of the National army's northward advance. Also, a certain elite unit of the National army, after lifting the siege of Rugao, has now arrived in the vicinity of Hai'an and established contact with the National army originally stationed in the town. The Communist forces near Huangqiao have been moving towards Qutang and Baimi for days, their purpose being to strengthen the forces on the Qutang-Hai'an line in order to prevent the National army from advancing west.

[Report from our Xinpu office, 15th] The National army in northern Jiangsu has made rapid progress since recovering Suqian. The vanguard forces have now arrived at places such as Dingji and Xinji, more than twenty li southwest of Shuyang County. The Communist army's Fourth Regiment, entrenched in the territory of Shuyang County, seeing the tense situation, has experienced a mutiny in one unit. The Communist army has imposed martial law in its controlled areas starting from the 10th, prohibiting people from passing through, and conscripting young men from house to house, establishing a reserve regiment in each district in preparation for civil war.

[Another Dispatch] The Lianhai Line, the eastern section of the Longhai Railway, added automatic express trains on the 15th of this month, running four times a day in each direction.

[United Press, this city, 16th] According to a senior military officer of the National army in northern Jiangsu: except for a section of about fifty li along the Longhai Railway east of Xuzhou, the remaining Communist forces in northern Jiangsu and northeastern Anhui Province have almost been completely surrounded by the National army. It is rumored that in the Battle of Sixian, the 8th Division of the Communist Eighth Route Army was virtually annihilated, so those currently in contact with the National army are only the 2nd and 7th Divisions and the 9th Column of the New Fourth Army. The 8th Division is an elite force of the Communist army, and this spring it captured eight counties from the National army. Although the Communist army still occupies a section of fifty li of the Longhai Railway as a retreat, the National army officer said: "That section of land is flooded, which will make the transportation of the Communist army's troops and supplies extremely difficult, so its importance has been reduced. And since the recovery of Lingbi, Wuhu, and Sixian, the National army has broken into the western part of this rectangular encirclement, which is conducive to reducing the Communist forces."

National Army Recovers Many Strongholds

[Central News Agency, Xuzhou, 16th] Huaiyin is the main stronghold of the Communist army, and they often harass the National army. The National army there was forced to counterattack, and at 10:00 AM on the 15th, they recovered Chenjiaji (13 kilometers southwest of Huaiyin), Dabao (3 kilometers north of Chenjiaji), and Wangjia Taoyuan (9 kilometers southwest of Huaiyin). They then continued to counterattack Xiaoyuezhen (3 kilometers southeast of Chenjiaji), Matouzhen (7 kilometers southwest of Huaiyin), and Yangzhuangzhen (5 kilometers west of Huaiyin). The Communist army resisted stubbornly and counterattacked the National army at Matouzhen six times, but was finally repelled. By 4:00 PM, all of the above strongholds had been completely recovered by the National army. In this battle, about a thousand Communist soldiers were captured.

[Central News Agency, Xuzhou, 16th] (1) The National army that recovered Siyang crossed the Grand Canal on the 14th and recovered Zhongxingji. The Communist army fled towards Shuyang. (2) The 9th Column of the Communist army, which had intruded into the Southern Xinjie (about 15 kilometers south of Siyang), was defeated by the National army on the 14th, and the area was recovered. The remaining Communist troops fled west towards Huaiyin.

National Army in Western Shandong Recovers Jining 5

[Central News Agency, Jinan, 16th] The National army recovered Jining on the morning of the 15th, which is the first city in western Shandong (west of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway).

[Central News Agency, Xuzhou, 16th] The Communist army's 9th Column in Jining, Shandong, suddenly attacked the National army on the 15th. The National army immediately counterattacked, and the Communist army was defeated and routed. The National army took the opportunity to recover Jining City. More than 600 Communist soldiers surrendered and handed over more than 1,000 rifles.

Bumper Autumn Harvest, Grain Prices Fall Universally; Economic Situation Bound to Change; Xu Kan Talks to Our Reporter 6

[Report from our Nanjing office, 16th] Minister Xu of the Ministry of Food met with our reporter at 5:00 PM on the 16th and made the following statement: "This year's autumn harvest has been bountiful in most parts of the country, and grain prices have fallen universally. However, because (1) the damage suffered by rural areas during the long eight-year war of resistance was extremely great, and has not yet returned to its original state in the short term; (2) in the disaster-stricken areas last year, due to the severe lack of manpower, animal power, fertilizer, and seeds, cultivation was not widespread; (3) in some areas with particularly abundant grain production, grain is currently being blockaded or destroyed, and transportation is also being destroyed or obstructed, making it difficult for the flow of grain to return to a state of equilibrium between surplus and deficiency; (4) before the war, the average amount of grain imported overseas each year was about 1.6 million tons, even in years of good harvest, it was around 1 million tons. Based on the above four points, with regard to the future grain situation, we sincerely hope that domestic transportation can be restored quickly so that areas with surplus or deficiency can be adjusted accordingly. We also hope that rice, wheat, and flour from abroad can be transported in as scheduled to enrich the people's food supply. In the coming months, it will be a season of falling grain prices, and grain prices in various places will continue to fall. We sincerely hope that wages and general prices can fall equally, then the economic situation will be greatly improved."

Communist Party Determined to Expand Civil War; Cadre Meeting Held in Northern Shaanxi; "Central Tasks" Determined for the Present 7

[Report from our Nanjing office, 16th] Since the Communist Party issued a general mobilization broadcast from Yan'an, there have been active movements in various counties in northern Shaanxi, and a cadre meeting was held to discuss the issue of internal unrest. The central tasks determined for the present are as follows: (1) war first, production second; (2) expand the conscription of young men; (3) strengthen "suppression of traitors," strictly check pedestrians, and eliminate "villains"; (4) crack down on war-resistant elements and enhance the belief in the inevitable victory of the civil war; (5) strengthen wartime organizations, such as stretcher teams, transportation teams, guerrilla teams, and small groups; (6) strengthen wartime education, such as propaganda and clearing the fields.

Ambassador Marshall Leaves Gu to Return to Nanjing; Wu and Zhang Visit the Ambassador to Exchange Views; Zhou Enlai Arrives in Shanghai, Return Date to Nanjing Undetermined 8

[Report from our Nanjing office, 16th] Special Envoy Marshall and his wife will leave Gu on the 17th to return to Nanjing. The political activities in the capital will be determined after Ambassador Marshall comes down the mountain. At 10:30 AM on the 16th, Wang Bingnan of the Communist delegation visited Ambassador Stuart. Wang told him that the current war situation is serious and that there is an urgent need to convene a military three-person group meeting to discuss the necessity of a truce as soon as possible. He also said: "If we proceed through the political path through an informal five-person group meeting, it will not be easy to obtain the most effective way to resolve the current critical situation." Ambassador Stuart believed that the military problem is serious, but if we do not start from the political path to achieve the goal of a truce, then the so-called "truce" is still not a long-term solution. The Ambassador still believes that convening an informal five-person group meeting is the appropriate method at present. Wang left at 12:00. At 11:00 AM, Pi Zonggan, a counselor from the Nationalist government, also visited the Ambassador. Pi told reporters that this visit was half public and half private, because Pi brought his paperwork with him. At 11:20 AM, Pi drove away himself. At 4:30 PM, Zhang Lisheng visited Ambassador Stuart, and at 5:00 PM, Wu Tiecheng also arrived, and Pi Zonggan was also present during the meeting with the Ambassador. They left successively at 6:45 PM. It is reported that the content of the conversation was that Ambassador Stuart first told about his conversation with Wang Bingnan, and then they exchanged opinions. The Ambassador seemed eager to find an appropriate way to promote this peace negotiation.

[Central News Agency, Guling, 16th] Chairman Chiang and his wife and Special Envoy Marshall and his wife revisited the Five Old Peaks at 5:00 PM on the afternoon of the 16th and had a picnic there. Marshall also had his first meeting with the Chairman after climbing Guling eight times. They returned with pleasure around 6:00 PM.

[Report from our Nanjing office, 16th] Zhou Enlai took a special plane to Shanghai from Nanjing Airport at 2:30 PM on the afternoon of the 16th. His secretary Zhang Wenjin and Communist Party spokesman Fan Changjiang and others accompanied him. In the evening, Wang Bingnan, spokesman for the Communist Party delegation, said that Zhou's stay in Shanghai was indefinite, and he would only return when the military three-person group meeting had a definite date to convene, which is also sufficient to show the Communist Party's stubborn attitude. Also, Zhou's trip will use the "masses'" order to suspend publication as a matter to negotiate with various parties.

Communist Army Uses Negotiations as an Excuse to Seek a Chance to Breathe 9

[Central News Agency, New York, 16th] The New York Times, according to what the American reporter stationed in Nanjing said, the Communist Party, in view of the recent military victories of the National army, wants to use Marshall to achieve a truce agreement, and said that there are signs that China has obtained a temporary peace. Yan'an is good at political warfare, and propaganda and obstruction are its most important weapons. Yan'an, in addition to using guerrilla tactics, is not prepared to meet the National army on the battlefield. After the National army achieved a surprising victory in the Northeast last time, Yan'an showed a clear tendency to negotiate, which seems to happen again. But even if any concrete results can be produced, or it is only a tactical concession. Past experience tells us that this is just a Communist trick. The newspaper said: "The advancement of national policy has not launched a full-scale offensive against Yan'an, its purpose is only to 'force the Communist Party to withdraw from the many occupied lands it seized after the Japanese army surrendered, so as to end the economic paralysis caused by this occupation.'"

Traitors Zhou Fohai, Ding Mocun, and Others; Five Major Traitors Escorted to Nanjing Yesterday; Each Person Looked Discouraged, With Regret of "Thinking of Those Years" 14

[Report from our Nanjing office, 16th] The five major traitors, including Zhou Fohai and Ding Mocun, who are considered to have "special characteristics" by all parties, were flown from Chongqing and escorted to Nanjing at 4:45 PM on the 16th. Because the news was confidential, very few people knew about it in advance. Our reporter waited at the airport for two hours before seeing China National Aviation Corporation passenger plane No. 38 descending. The personnel responsible for the escort first deployed guards on the field. After the cabin door was opened, two small buses and two large trucks specially prepared by the Bureau of Investigation and Statistics drove up. Ding Mocun first stood at the cabin door, looking gloomy, wearing a gray gabardine long gown, white silk trousers, gray cotton black shoes, with a sallow complexion. Then Zhou Fohai also appeared. He was taller than Ding Mocun. According to observers on the field, he was much thinner than in the era of the puppet government, and his demeanor was also greatly discouraged, seeming to imply "I have also seen your end." Zhou was wearing a gray cloth long gown, white trousers, light red short socks, and black shoes. When getting off the plane, Ding was in front, and Zhou was second. Zhou entered the car box at a rapid pace. Next was Luo Junqiang, wearing a blue-gray gauze short gown and trousers, holding a raincoat. The three traitors rode in the same car. Then there were Ma, Yang (names unknown), and a maid riding in another car. There were also several men and women following, their facial expressions were very nervous, presumably they were their family members and followers. It is learned that they talked from time to time in the plane, their mood was discouraged, especially Zhou seemed to be unable to overcome the feelings of today and past, the luxury of when he invested in "Wang's regime" in the past and being a prisoner in Nanjing again. After getting off the plane, they were taken directly to the detention center at No. 19 Ninghai Road. Our reporter went to explore their life in the thunderstorm in the evening, but did not get to enter for a visit, but saw that the interior was a Western-style residence, with bright electric lights and open glass windows. The light and air were much better than the residences of the petty bourgeoisie. According to inquiries, Zhou and Luo lived in the same room, with two beds and a table in the room. Ding, Ma, Yang and their adjutant lived in one room, and the nurse and maid lived in one room. No one has visited after entering the prison. The guarding police officers all smiled and told that Zhou and others were very silent and did not say much, but their uneasy demeanor showed the regret of "thinking of those years" and "a single wrong step." It is also heard that Zhou and others will soon be transferred to the Capital High Court for trial.

Yellow River Water Level Continues to Rise, Breaking Records Since the Beginning of the Republic 21

[Central News Agency, Zhengzhou, 16th] The water level of the Yellow River in Shaan County briefly dropped on the afternoon of the 14th, but rose again on the 15th. The water level reached 295.0506 meters, with a flow rate of 10,000 cubic meters per second. The water flow from Lanzhou is estimated to reach Shaan County in two days, Huayuankou in one day, and Shahe in two days. The water level in Lanzhou has already broken records since the beginning of the Republic. The bridges in both the north and south of Zhoukou are preparing to be destroyed in case the water level rises again, in order to save Zhoukou from danger.

Wuxi Command Post Established: Commanders of Various Suppression and Joint Defense Zones Appointed; Bandit Surrender to be Organized at Xukou 24

[Our newspaper, Wuxi, 16th] The Wuxi Command Post of the Capital Garrison Headquarters was officially established on the 16th. At 10:00 AM, Lieutenant General Chen Daqing, concurrently Director of the Command Post, and Major General Mao Sen, Chief of Staff, met with the press and made a statement. The jurisdiction of the post includes 27 counties, including Guangde, Yixing, Gaochun, Changshu, and Wuxi. It is divided into the Maoshan, Taihu, Jiangsu-Zhejiang-Anhui Border Area, Yangcheng Lake Four Suppression Zones, and Changshu-Danyang-Yangzhong, Wuxi-Chengjiang, Pudong, and Chongming Four Joint Defense Zones. The commanders of the various suppression and joint defense zones have all been appointed and have been established separately. In addition, in the villages of Huazhuang Township and Sunjiali Village in southern Xiang, dozens of bandits suddenly appeared recently, robbing people and demanding ransoms. After receiving the report, County Magistrate Xu Jianruo dispatched Security Team Attaché Hu Shaomei to lead a suppression team to the villages. They opened fire in the village on the night of the 15th. Attaché Hu was injured in the face, and the bandits fled into the night. Seven suspected bandits, including Wang Aju, were arrested and taken to the city for investigation.

[Our newspaper, Wuxi correspondence] Since the authorities sent Yang Yanbin as the commissioner for pacification of the lake bandits on Taihu's Pingtai Mountain and engaged in pacification work, Yang immediately sent his former subordinate Tang Guiye to the lake to make contact. Because they all wished to surrender, Yang decided to visit the bandit stronghold on Pingtai Mountain to meet with the bandit leader and discuss the procedures for their incorporation. At 6:00 AM on the 13th, Yang, together with Dai Junying, Chief of Staff of the City Defense Command, accompanied Tang Guiye and more than ten guards, departed from the city. At 2:00 PM, they arrived at Wutangmen and left the guards there to wait. Dai, Yang, and two others took a small gunboat and sailed to Pingtai Mountain. At the time, the person in charge of the bandit group, Hui Bingnan, was not on the mountain, as he had gone to meet at the invitation of Duo Hongde, Deputy Commander of the Taihu Suppression Zone. Zhang Kuan and a staff officer of the bandit group, Li, welcomed them and went up the mountain. They negotiated the procedures for the incorporation and reached a satisfactory result. Zhang and others stated that they had the consent of the leader, Hui Bingnan, and were willing to wait for orders to gather and accept the incorporation. It was agreed that the incorporation would take place at Xukou, near Wusimudu. After Yang and others returned to Wuxi, they reported to Chief of Staff Mao, who confirmed the date and ordered them to comply. The bandit group stated that they would guarantee navigational safety from that day forward, so that ships could resume sailing. That night, Yang and others stayed on the mountain and returned to the city the next morning. They had already reported the situation to Chief of Staff Mao.

Minister Xie Instructs Prosecutors and Judges in Jiangsu, Stating the Judicial System Should Immediately Implement Chairman's New, Fast, and Practical Principles 25

[Our newspaper, Suzhou, 16th] Minister of Justice Xie, at 10:00 AM on the 16th, attended the joint weekly memorial service of the High Court and District Court, and addressed the assembled three hundred prosecutors and judges. He said: Reconstruction work, especially the judiciary, is the most important area, because the punishment of traitors and the resolution of civil and criminal disputes are all related to the national principles and social justice. The units below the Jiangsu High Court have achieved considerable results in the past year, but they are not yet perfect and require continued efforts from everyone. He also hoped that they would strive to implement the three words "New," "Fast," and "Practical" as demonstrated in the Chairman's speech, so that changing customs and turning weakness into strength would not be difficult to achieve. As for his explanation: "New" means adapting to the times, constantly striving for self-improvement, innovating daily, and evolving with the times. "Fast" means taking the psychology of the parties involved in litigation as your own, empathizing with others, and handling cases quickly. "Practical" means taking responsibility for judging cases, being down-to-earth, and handling cases impartially. He hoped that everyone would eliminate long-standing malpractices and strive to act diligently in all three areas. Xie continued to encourage his colleagues to take on responsibilities and endure hardships, and to bring glory to the entire judicial system. The weekly meeting ended at 12:00 PM. He then went to the Lion Grove for lunch and visited famous gardens such as Humble Administrator's Garden. He took a special train, the Xishan, back to Shanghai and then Hangzhou at 4:30 PM in the afternoon.

Suzhou Regiment Management District to Conduct Conscription; Commander Du Xu Arrives Yesterday 26

[Our newspaper, Suzhou, 16th] The Conscription Bureau of the Ministry of National Defense plans to implement a conscription system along the Nanjing-Shanghai line and has ordered the commanders of various division regiment management districts to be responsible for its implementation. Conscription is one of the main tasks.

Monster Discovered in Beiping, Face Like a Spider, All Features Present 27

[United Press, Beiping, 15th]

According to reports, a monster with a face like a spider has been discovered in a temple west of Xibianmen, twelve miles west of Beiping. It is about the size of an apple, with a black body and a white face, and all its facial features are present. The front four legs are long, and the rear four legs are small. It is said that it can also spin silk, but it prefers to live in the shade of trees. It has only been a few days since this spider was born, and it is not yet clear whether it has grown teeth. This monster was discovered by a monk in a peach tree, and he placed the spider, along with the tree branch, in a large bottle to await scientific research.

Executive Yuan Relief and Rehabilitation Administration and Ministry of Food to Exchange Grain; Discussions Reach Concrete Stage; Contract to be Signed Soon 30

[Our newspaper, Nanjing, 16th] The important decision announced by Director Jiang of the Executive Yuan Relief and Rehabilitation Administration (ERRRA) at the ERRRA work review meeting on the 7th, regarding the negotiation of exchange methods with the Ministry of Food, has gradually reached a concrete stage. The two parties will sign a contract and begin implementation in the coming days. The contract content roughly states that starting in September, the two parties will exchange 50,000 tons of grain each month, in order to save time and expenses and exchange what they have for what they need. The exchange areas for the grain will be the four provinces of Hunan, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Zhejiang. The ERRRA will deliver all the grain to the Shanghai branch of the Yangtze River Grain Storage and Transportation Bureau of the Ministry of Food in Shanghai, and the Ministry of Food will deliver the grain to the Grain Management Offices in each province. The distribution of the grain will be handled separately.

Over 100,000 Taels of Opium from Hubei Publicly Burned in Hankou 33

[Our newspaper, Hankou, 16th] A total of 108,856 taels of opium received by the Wuhan District Committee for Handling Confiscated Materials and the Hubei Provincial Government were publicly burned at Zhongshan Park starting at 1:50 PM today. At this point, the poisonous substance, valued at over 20 billion, was completely destroyed, and all who heard of it praised the action.

Declaration of the Second National Congress of the Youth League (Continued from the Third Edition on the 14th) 36

(II) Here, we must also express our frank and sincere opinions on the current party issues in the country.

We believe that the ideal of communism and the Principle of People's Livelihood in the Three Principles of the People, which we believe in, differ only in philosophical foundation and implementation methods. However, the goal of transforming this economically deformed society into an economically equal and common society is the same. However, it is universally recognized by all Chinese and foreign people that Marxism, which originated in Western societies where capitalism has become deeply rooted after the Industrial Revolution, cannot be overly applied to China, which is lagging behind in industrial development. As for the discrepancy between the words and deeds of the Chinese Communist Party, it is even more obvious. The Communist Party used to call for resistance against Japan, but in reality, it used the opportunity of resistance to develop its power; it shouted for unity, but in reality, it attempted to divide the territory and undermine the unity of our country; today, it shouts for democracy, but in reality, it practices class dictatorship in the liberated areas it has opened up. From the advancement in the south and the invasion of the Northeast to the attack on Datong, it has never stopped its ambition to seize territory and attack cities, and its reckless actions that harm the country and the people. We really do not understand what their intentions are. What we especially and absolutely oppose is the Chinese Communist Party teaching people not to love their country and teaching people to diminish humanity. It is clear that the Communist Party disregards the interests of the country, does not hesitate to undermine our country's international status, and eliminates our nation's self-esteem. The inherent morality of the Chinese nation lies in loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, trustworthiness, righteousness, and peace. The reason why China was able to resist the aggression of Japan and obtain the final victory was not due to the superiority of science or organization in a few people, but due to the potential of the various inherent moral national spirits left by our ancestors. The Chinese Communist Party does not hesitate to destroy it ruthlessly. No matter what country or nation, it is especially necessary for its citizens to have the spirit of independence and freedom in order to establish itself in today's world. The Chinese Communist Party does not hesitate to ruthlessly destroy the most valuable cultural heritage of the country and the nation. Not only are we youths of the Three Principles of the People firmly opposed to it, but even the youths of all levels of society in the country, even those who have already joined the Chinese Communist Party, may not be able to bear it.

What we have always expected from the Chinese Communist Party is that they will abide by their promises made in the early days of the War of Resistance to support Chairman Chiang and thoroughly realize the Three Principles of the People, promote nationalization, integrate their armed forces into the country's military, and become a legitimate political party in order to promote the implementation of constitutional government. If they can win the sympathy of the people for their socialist policies and urge the government to implement them, then we, the youth of the Three Principles of the People, who originally regard the implementation of the Principle of People's Livelihood as our great duty, do not want to oppose them. Based on our conscience and our reason, we ask the many youths of the Chinese Communist Party to consider deeply, not to be intoxicated by a few ambitious people, and even more not to be coerced by dark violence and mislead the country and themselves. Only in this way can they be considered youths of the Republic of China and be worthy of being descendants of the Yellow Emperor.

In addition, we would also like to state here our opinions on other parties other than the Chinese Communist Party. We believe that in accordance with the great road of the Three Principles of the People and the grand plan of the National Father's revolution for our country, when the time comes for constitutional government, any party, as long as it does not violate the Three Principles of the People and does not plot to harm the Republic of China, can obtain legitimate existence and protection. The Three Principles of the People state that the country is owned by the people and politics is shared by the people. In the political thought of this century, this glorious and immortal proposition will inevitably be protected by all enlightened people. There is absolutely no reason for a fair and just political party to oppose the fundamental proposition of the Three Principles of the People. The policies advocated by the various parties now, although there are some differences, have not been able to escape the scope of the Three Principles of the People. The Chinese Nationalist Party has a glorious history of holding the Three Principles of the People revolution to save the country for fifty years, and today it has made great contributions to the Republic of China. At a time when the Chinese Nationalist Party is leading the people of the country to resist Japanese imperialism and is about to realize constitutional government, people from all parties have a patriotic conscience. They will inevitably cherish the past hard work of the Nationalist Party and accept the sincerity of the Nationalist Party to cooperate sincerely with all parties in order to achieve the goal of peaceful nation-building. If the interests of the party are placed above the interests of the country, and the morality of the political party is placed below the strength of the political party, it is not the demeanor that a politician should have. Especially for political parties in a democratic government, they must have the spirit of independence and autonomy and the magnanimity of being open and aboveboard. They must not be considered the outer circle of the Communist Party and speak for the Communist Party in vain. If their content and spirit are manipulated by the Communist Party and cannot be autonomous, and their actions and speeches are dominated by the Communist Party and they lose their independent purpose, then it does not conform to the spirit of today's democratic politics. We, the youth of the Three Principles of the People, not only feel sorry for them, but also feel disappointed in them.

(III) Based on the above-mentioned domestic enthusiasm and the various domestic political parties, we want to state our belief in the Three Principles of the People and our views on the current state affairs.

We deeply believe that the Three Principles of the People is not only the great road to save China, but also the truth to transform the lives of all mankind. The Three Principles of the People start from humanitarianism and focus on the survival of all mankind. It explores all the spirits of freedom, equality, and fraternity, and is guided by scientific thought. The Three Principles of the People is a combination of nationalism, democracy, and the Principle of People's Livelihood. We, the followers of the Three Principles of the People, naturally oppose fascism and imperialism. We cannot agree with the doctrine of class dictatorship that originates from materialism and ignores political freedom. We believe that to save today's chaotic China, we can only adhere to the Three Principles of the People and strive to implement the Three Principles of the People. Similarly, to save today's chaotic world, we can only seek a reasonable solution to the three major problems of human economy, politics, and nation based on the principles of the Three Principles of the People. First, internationally, we advocate faithfully abiding by the United Nations Charter, uniting all countries in the world, and solving all the urgent problems that need to be solved in a permanent way. All outdated ideas that attempt to use strong military force to dominate the world, as well as those that oppose racial equality, the freedom of the people, and economic interdependence, should not be allowed to exist. China, in its current chaotic situation, should promote the consistent spirit of justice and reason of our Chinese nation, fulfill our obligations as a member of the United Nations, to promote the cooperation of friendly countries, to implement our common war goals, to prevent the revival of strong politics, that is, to permanently eliminate the recurrence of war. The Three Principles of the People is the strength we rely on, and it is the unity of 450 million people. We must resolutely strive to realize the truth.

Secondly, domestically, we believe that today's China has entered a new era of constitutional government. It is the eve of the completion of the country by the people of the country, and it is also the beginning of difficult creation. The Peaceful Nation-Building Outline, etc., jointly decided by the government to convene the Political Consultative Conference of various political parties for the sake of peaceful nation-building, must be sincerely implemented throughout the country in order to achieve the goal of peaceful unification and democracy desired by the whole country.

However, what we want to point out painfully is that it has been a full year since the victory of the War of Resistance Against Japan, but why has the suffering of our compatriots deepened instead, the worries of the country have increased instead, the glory of victory has become increasingly dim, and the martyrs who sacrificed in the War of Resistance Against Japan have not been comforted? The creation of this humiliating phenomenon is really because the unity of our country has been threatened, the nation-building plan has not been realized, and also because the Three Principles of the People have not been implemented. Therefore, we want to awaken all compatriots in the country to truly recognize: (1) the necessity of supporting unity, (2) the necessity of implementing nation-building, and even more, to urge the government to fulfill its responsibility to implement the Three Principles of the People.

First: We must uphold national unity, which is an essential element of nation-building. It is the guarantee of social stability and the freedom of the people, and it is also a prerequisite for the implementation of democratic nation-building. We advocated the three major goals of peace, unity, and stability at the time of the end of the War of Resistance, and we have worked hard to use peaceful negotiation methods to make the Chinese Communist Party abandon its attempts to divide the country by armed secession and achieve true national unity. The government's consistent policy is precisely the urgent prayer of our compatriots and the unanimous support of our youth across the country; however, in the past year, despite the continuous negotiations, the Communist Party has always insisted on its concept of self-owned armed forces and feudal secession, constantly attacking the National Army and expanding its territory, and must destroy the unity of the country's military orders and political orders completely, creating the phenomenon of "a country within a country" and "an army outside the National Army," and even the traffic has been cut off section by section, the economy has been divided everywhere, and the restoration and relief work cannot be carried out. If this continues, not only will the people not be able to live, but the country will not be a country. In order to maintain the results of victory and safeguard the survival of the country, all our youth should not hesitate to sacrifice freedom, sacrifice life, sacrifice everything, to ensure national unity. It is determined that the urgency of saving the country today. For acts that undermine unity, our youth across the country must unite the will and strength of the entire nation, exert public opinion, and impose sanctions.

Second: We must implement the national construction strategy. Resistance and nation-building were originally national policies that went hand in hand. Immediately after the victory of the War of Resistance, nation-building should begin immediately. In the past year, it has been delayed and wasted. It must not be delayed any longer. We must do our best, overcome all difficulties, and speed up the progress of construction work. (The following text turns to the third edition)

Editorial

Molotov's Astonishing Speech 37

Just as the vigorous debate in international circles sparked by American Henry Wallace's speech was beginning to subside, Soviet Foreign Minister Molotov, at the Paris Peace Conference's Committee on Italian Political and Territorial Questions, delivered a lengthy speech, lasting over sixty minutes. While ostensibly focused on the Trieste issue, the speech's scope was broad, and its underlying meaning demanded careful consideration. Regarding the veto issue, Molotov stated that rejecting or eliminating the veto would only aid those attempting to establish an Anglo-American bloc. Ignoring the Soviet Union in the pursuit of peace would be dangerous. The United Nations, if seeking to safeguard peace without Soviet participation, or even in opposition to the Soviet Union, was bound to fail. Any attempt aimed at eliminating the veto should be regarded as a prelude to a new war and rejected. He also asserted that 19th-century democratic principles were no longer suited to the 20th century, citing Greece and Bulgaria as examples of two different forms of democracy. While elections in Greece may have been marred by fraud and foreign interference, the Soviet Union had exerted no pressure on Bulgaria's referendum. Molotov's speech thus bordered on a veiled challenge. As Molotov's first speech since returning to Paris from Moscow, its significance was undoubtedly profound.

Regarding the Trieste issue, Molotov advocated rejecting the drafts proposed by Britain, the United States, or France, and fully adopting the Soviet plan, which outlined the following key points: (1) The Free Territory of Trieste should be designated as a neutral and demilitarized zone; (2) All foreign troops should withdraw from the Free Territory of Trieste within thirty days after the entry into force of the treaty of peace with Italy; (3) The Free Territory of Trieste should be economically integrated with Yugoslavia; (4) The government of the Free Territory should be responsible to the People's Assembly of the territory; (5) All Italian citizens residing in the territory, with the exception of those who supported the Italian Fascist regime, held official positions in the Fascist Party, served in the Italian police, were government officials who came to the territory from Italy after 1921, or were war criminals, should be granted citizenship in the territory; (6) An Allied Council composed of Britain, the United States, the Soviet Union, and France should be formed to organize the interim government of the Free Territory upon the treaty's entry into force, and should solicit the opinions of local democratic groups and parties; (7) The special responsibility of the interim government should be to convene elections for the People's Assembly within three months, forming the formal government of the Free Territory. On the surface, this plan appeared fair and just, but it concealed the following problems: (1) The plan did not specify a time limit for the existence of the Free Territory, unlike the drafts proposed by Britain, the United States, and France, which stipulated a period of ten years; (2) The establishment and existence of the Free Territory would be completely detached from the control of the United Nations; (3) The acquisition of citizenship by Italian citizens in the territory was subject to certain restrictions, effectively disenfranchising tens of thousands of Italians. As a result, Yugoslavs would gain control in the territory, and since this arrangement was not time-limited and the People's Assembly would be the highest decision-making body, the People's Assembly established under the Soviet plan could very well pass legislation annexing the Free Territory of Trieste to Yugoslavia. Thus, upon closer examination, the plan appeared to greatly benefit Yugoslavia. From the perspective of an objective observer, resolving the delicate and complex Trieste issue through this plan would not be as straightforward as simply annexing the territory to Yugoslavia.

We cannot deny that Molotov's speech was filled with vigor, presenting an interesting contrast to Wallace's weak and powerless remarks. In summary, the key point of Molotov's speech was to

intimidate generally weak-willed individuals, forcing them to unconditionally accept all of the Soviet Union's policies. As the Soviet Foreign Minister, Molotov repeatedly mentioned Britain, France, and the Anglo-American bloc in his speech, as if those capitalist countries were indeed establishing anti-Soviet states. When it came to the democratic system, Molotov candidly stated that only the Soviet system was a thoroughly modern democracy that could be implemented in other countries, while the British concept of democracy was outdated. All of this, if uttered by German or Italian propaganda ministers before the downfall of the Nazis and Fascists, would not have been much different!

Molotov brought up the Munich Agreement, which he abhorred, a matter that everyone should certainly remember. However, people might also recall the signing of the German-Soviet Non-Aggression Pact on the eve of the outbreak of World War II in Europe. If the Munich Agreement unleashed a rabid Nazi dog, wouldn't the Moscow Pact signed by Molotov and Ribbentrop be akin to instigating that rabid dog to bite people? Let's forget about this unpleasant matter. Sincere cooperation and joint efforts to create world peace would be the best course of action.

Molotov's speech bluntly pointed out that the maintenance of world peace requires accepting the Soviet viewpoint, which is "Soviet Peace" (Pax Sovietica). In other words, all policies that differ from the Soviet viewpoint should be abandoned, and only the Soviet viewpoint is correct. This is truly a "world domination" centered on the Soviet Union. If the peace won at the cost of countless lives were to be built on the foundation of such a Pax Sovietica, then the heroic souls on the Pacific desert islands, in the North African deserts, on the beaches of Normandy, and on the entire Chinese battlefield would surely weep. This is an era that requires decisions! Humanity is also facing the eve of a new historical stage!

Resolution Demanding the Recovery of Hong Kong 38

The Shanghai Municipal Council passed a resolution yesterday, requesting the government to negotiate the recovery of Hong Kong, Macau, and other territories ceded or leased under unequal treaties. This resolution not only represents the views of the four million people of Shanghai, but also the unanimous desire of our entire nation of four hundred million people!

The unequal treaties previously signed between China and various countries began with the Treaty of Nanking after the Opium War, and the cession of Hong Kong was a product of the Treaty of Nanking, along with the opening of five treaty ports. Therefore, the recovery of ceded and leased territories should begin with Hong Kong.

Britain should return Hong Kong and Kowloon to China. This is an obligation that cannot be delayed, both legally and practically. During the war, the leaders of the three major powers, China, Britain, and the United States, met in Cairo to discuss long-term plans for the Far East, and in principle unanimously agreed to return Hong Kong and Kowloon to China. US senators criticized Britain for its reluctance to easily give up Hong Kong. Even British authorities have stated that once the time is ripe, they will negotiate with China to discuss the return of Hong Kong. Stephen, the new British Ambassador to China, also solemnly stated when he departed from Britain to assume his new post: "Britain has no ambition in China other than commerce; it earnestly hopes that China will become a strong, stable, and unified country. The British government will do its utmost to assist China within the greatest possible scope to ensure that China becomes a strong and unified country." Everyone believed that with the unfolding of a new chapter in Sino-British relations, the stains on the diplomatic history of the two countries could be completely erased.

The British rule of Hong Kong and the lease of Kowloon to Britain are both the result of Britain's past aggression against China. Now that Britain regards China as an ally, and during the war, the two countries fought shoulder to shoulder against aggression, their friendship has been strengthened through the crucible of blood. Therefore, at this moment, not only for China's sake, but especially for Britain's sake, it is most timely to eliminate the vestiges of past British imperialism and to bridge the gap between the peoples of China and Britain.

Since the Labour Party came to power in Britain, it has adopted enlightened policies both internally and externally. Prime Minister Attlee has allowed India to become independent and announced the withdrawal of British troops from Egypt, earning worldwide acclaim. Recently, US Secretary of Commerce Wallace delivered a speech criticizing Britain for adopting imperialist policies in the Near East, which aroused deep indignation among the British people. This shows that Britain today no longer admits to maintaining an imperialist style. Accordingly, Britain's expression of following its past imperialist path in the Far East makes it even more necessary to return Hong Kong and Kowloon to China.

However, Hong Kong and Kowloon have been under British rule for a century, and negotiations with our country on the return issue will take some time technically. But we must not allow the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to keep delaying the matter. Some people in Britain may still hope to postpone it, but our people have the right to urge the government to start negotiations for recovery as soon as possible. Hong Kong does occupy a very important position in Far Eastern trade. Our demand for the recovery of Hong Kong and Kowloon is to maintain the integrity of our country's territorial sovereignty, and there is no other purpose. Moreover, we can also advocate that after Hong Kong is recovered, it should still be used as a free port for international trade, making it a trade center in the Far East and Southeast Asia. This is beneficial to both China and Britain, and to the world. We support this resolution of the Shanghai Municipal Council and demand that the government attach importance to this resolution representing public opinion.

Transformation of Modern American Thought 39

Professor Fei, in a speech at Tongji University the other day, raised two important issues: first, world peace; and second, educational reform. From Professor Fei's perspective, we can see the transformation of modern American thought. Because Professor Fei himself admits that what he said is not only his personal opinion, but the opinion of the majority of modern Americans.

Regarding world peace, Professor Fei believes that in order to avoid war, it is necessary to establish a world police system. The police represent a kind of power, and the law cannot be enforced without power behind it. He acknowledged that this construction work is very difficult, but inevitable. Someone asked him if he believed in "power politics," and he said it depended on how it was interpreted. Just as Shanghai needs to maintain public order, it has set up a police force, but the police cannot be regarded as power politics.

Recently, after reading many speeches by American political authorities, scholars, and journalists, and observing many military preparations and demonstrations in the United States, we feel that behind these speeches and actions, there is indeed a new view of international relations that is latent among most Americans. Few people can say that Americans today deliberately want war and are unwilling to have peace, but their thinking is completely different from what it was after World War I. After the last war, they believed that peace could be achieved by peaceful means. After this war, while they still adopt peaceful means on the one hand, they actively prepare military force on the other hand. They clearly want to use military force to compel peace. This is a drastic change in the thinking of the average American.

If the world powers can, in the aftermath of this war, work together with one heart and mind, and build a world police system, the world will not be difficult to achieve peace. However, suspicion and fear arise between them, especially the increasingly acute relations between the United States and the Soviet Union. Since the United States and the Soviet Union cannot cooperate, and in order to demand world peace, everyone believes that the world police force is necessary. As a result, both countries intend to expand their own military strength to independently build the world police system. Even if their ultimate goal is peace, their current behavior seems to be tainted with the color of hegemony. The stronger the color, the deeper the suspicion, and the more difficult it is to cooperate. This is the crux of all the difficulties in the current international situation!

Regarding educational reform, Professor Fei gave us a surprising message. He said that many American educators advocate that students who study natural sciences and engineering should also take courses in social sciences, philosophy, and literature in the future. He also pointed out that several famous schools have extended the length of students' studies in order to complete the work of this educational ideal, such as the most famous Massachusetts Institute of Technology, which has been changed from four years to five years.

This reform movement originated from a new idea. Some American intellectuals, especially the experts who participated in the successful research of the atomic bomb, believe that the research on the relationship between "things and things" has reached an amazing progress, while the research on the relationship between "people and people" remains the same. But unless the latter research can catch up with the former research, scientific progress may destroy mankind itself! He pointed out that there are two aspects in the world of learning, one is Confucius, and the other is Einstein. Confucius' learning is about "people and people," and Einstein's learning is about "things and things." In today's terms, Confucius' philosophy may have many aspects that are not suitable for modern times, but his basic spirit is the most urgent need at present.

Standing in the position of the Chinese people, we feel that Professor Fei and the general American educators' new understanding is an unprecedented innovation for the American education system, and it provides us with a high-minded foresight for the Chinese education system. Chinese scientific research, in an era when professors can hardly maintain a minimum standard of living, is of course out of the question, and there is absolutely no danger of knowing too much. However, in the past ten years or so, the government authorities have developed a prejudice, valuing students who study science and engineering, and despising students who study literature, philosophy, and social sciences. For example, in each overseas study examination, the number of the latter is only one or two, and nine out of ten send the former. This prejudice and biased policy is unreasonable in principle. In the future, Chinese education, because of the urgent needs of the times, must not abandon scientific research, or even be in a reactionary and backward state. However, balanced development, without bias or discrimination, is at least the most sound way to cultivate young people. Our government authorities plan how to create a large number of "technical talents," and rarely plan how to create a large number of true and complete "people"! Our educators also advocate "scientific education" all day long, and rarely advocate "spiritual education" that can promote scientific application and scientific use! Professor Fei's remarks can also be regarded as a mountain stone for our future education.

The two issues of world peace and educational reform are interrelated. If the world is to achieve peace, human beings must help each other; and if human beings are to help each other, the majority of people in the world must thoroughly understand the relationship between people and people and understand each other. We hope that the United States will strive for educational reform in the process of transforming the two ideas, and avoid the starting point for aggression and domination; and on the Soviet side, we especially hope that the same transformation of educational ideas will also occur.

Turkish Fleet Enters the Aegean Sea; Relations Improve Between Egypt and Turkey After Egyptian King's Visit; Rumor of a Military Alliance Between the US, Britain, and Turkey 41

[Agence France-Presse, Istanbul, 15th] It has been officially announced that the Turkish fleet is scheduled to sail from Smyrna to the Aegean Sea tomorrow for naval exercises. It is unknown whether the British and American fleets, which are also conducting exercises in the Aegean Sea at the same time, will meet. According to Turkish officials, the three fleets may not sail in single file through the Dardanelles Strait, as such a move would be too blatant a political action against the Soviet Union.

[Agence France-Presse, Cairo, 15th] Egyptian government sources recently stated that after the recent visit of Egyptian King Farouk to Turkey, it is expected that relations between the two countries will have new developments in the shortest possible time. Although King Farouk's visit was informal in nature, Egyptian Prime Minister Nuqrashi Pasha issued a public statement to the press, strongly stating that King Farouk's visit to Turkey will have a satisfactory impact on relations between the two countries. In addition, King Farouk's inspection tour in the Red Sea area also visited Yanbu, which will also improve relations between Egypt and Saudi Arabia. Furthermore, Britain is very interested in the possibility of improved relations between Egypt and Turkey. In addition, the dispute between Turkey and Syria over the issue of the Alexandretta region may also be resolved through Egyptian mediation.

[Agence France-Presse, Cairo, 16th] The London correspondent of the Egyptian newspaper "Al-Misri" reports that if the negotiations between the Soviet Union and Turkey on revising the status of the Turkish Dardanelles Strait fail, Britain may propose that Britain, the United States, Greece, and Turkey conclude a military alliance. As for Egypt, it does not need to openly participate in such an alliance, because according to the Anglo-Egyptian Treaty, Egypt follows Britain's lead. According to the four-nation alliance plan, the land and air forces will be under the command of the United States, the navy will be under the command of Britain, and the headquarters will be located in Ankara, with supply stations in Beirut. This Turkish plan has not yet been confirmed.

US and British Representatives Firmly Advocate the Establishment of a Free State in Trieste; Should Be Separated from Direct Relations with Italy and Yugoslavia; It is Feared That the Peace Conference Will Be Difficult to Conclude Before the UN General Assembly 42

[Our Report] London, 16th Broadcast: The Committee on Italian Political and Territorial Questions held a meeting in Paris today to discuss the Trieste issue. British and American representatives reiterated their determination that Trieste should be separated from Italy and Yugoslavia, and also from the political conspiracies of any country.

[United Press, Paris, 16th] US Democratic Senator Connally today demanded that the Peace Conference establish a truly Free State of Trieste, not dependent on Yugoslavia or Italy. Connally further cited the principles agreed upon by the Council of Foreign Ministers regarding Trieste, stating that for the sake of peace, these agreements should be respected. "We must make Trieste a symbol of world peace and security." Earlier, Yugoslav Deputy Prime Minister Kardelj delivered a speech in the Italian Political Committee for an hour, claiming that Western powers were attempting to "draw a great iron curtain in the Mediterranean region." The Slavic bloc launched a movement to allow Yugoslavia to have control over the Free Territory of Trieste. The opposition of the United States and Britain to the Slavic demands is only to protect their rights in the Mediterranean. Their motives are neither concerned with the people of Trieste nor concerned with the people of Italy. According to Kardelj, he supports the Yugoslav proposal to have Trieste's customs and foreign affairs attached to Yugoslavia, while the Trieste government will be jointly established by the Four Powers Committee.

[United Press, Paris, 15th] The Paris Peace Conference has now entered its eighth week, but less than one-third of the work has been completed. The biggest disputes at present are two points: one is the Italian issue, and the other is the border dispute between Greece and Albania. The situation is tense and is about to reach the brink. Therefore, it seems highly unlikely that the work of the Paris Peace Conference can be concluded before the UN General Assembly convenes on October 23. These two issues are not only difficult for the Peace Conference itself, but also pose a crisis in the relationship between the Soviet Union and Western countries. The fate of the Free Port of Trieste is the biggest obstacle to the Peace Conference, and this issue has caused repeated twists and turns in the Four Powers Foreign Ministers Conference this spring. After the Four Powers finally agreed to designate the port as a free port, a small committee was formed to plan the detailed plan for the future establishment of the government of Trieste. However, as soon as this subcommittee met, its handling was tricky due to differences of opinion between the Soviet Union and the United States, Britain, and France. The same situation also occurred in the Paris Peace Conference. In short, the United States, Britain, France, and their countries all agree that Trieste should be international in nature, and its administrator should be appointed by the United Nations. Also, Trieste should be equally detached from direct relations with Italy and Yugoslavia. The administrator has broad powers in the free territory of the port. However, the Soviet plan proposed by Molotov wants a people's assembly to be elected by all the people of the port, and the administrative power of the port should be largely granted to this people's assembly. As for the power of the administrator, it should be strictly limited and not be responsible to the Security Council, but to the Four Powers. As for the issue of the Albanian-Greek border, there are also differences of opinion between the Eastern and Western blocs. The previous Four Powers Foreign Ministers Conference decided that representatives from Albania and Greece should present their views at the Peace Conference. At present, this dispute is being handled by the Peace Conference's Bulgarian Territorial Committee. Although Albania was formerly an enemy country, it demanded that the entire region of Western Thrace be assigned to Albania so as to obtain an outlet to the Aegean Sea. It has now formally proposed an amendment to the boundary, but Greece only requests a slight modification along the current boundary. The country did not formally propose a boundary amendment until last Friday.

Newspaper Report from the New York Scripps-Howard Group: Calls for Wallace to Step Down; Truman's Approval of Speech Revealed 48

This matter will be addressed by the Americans themselves in response to Wallace, it is said.

[Report from our newspaper] Broadcast from San Francisco, 16th: Today, the New York Scripps-Howard newspapers published an editorial stating that Wallace has caused too much trouble for Truman and his cabinet. He should no longer use his position in the cabinet to conduct "harmful activities." He should resign from the position of Secretary of Commerce; otherwise, he should be forced to take this step. The newspaper's Washington correspondent, Childs, described the process of President Truman's approval of Wallace's speech, stating that Truman never had the full text of the speech in hand. When Wallace went to the White House, he hastily read out several sections of the speech, which were not anti-British, but supported American foreign policy. Truman said, "We all agree on this point; I certainly agree." Later, after the State Department received the initial draft of the speech, Deputy Secretary of State Clayton tried to persuade Truman to cancel the speech. However, the initial draft was already being transmitted by radio, so President Truman and his advisors believed that canceling the speech would have even more adverse effects.

US Drafts New Military Program Based on Atomic Bombs and Other Weapons (Arctic Ocean as the First Line of Defense for the Americas) 49

[United Press Washington, 15th] The Department of the Army revealed today that the American military authorities have abolished the military program of the Second World War and replaced it with a new military program. This new program, based on atomic bombs, radio-controlled missiles, and electronic inventions, has been drafted by the General Staff and has begun to be taught at the Army War College in Washington and the Command and General Staff School in Fort Leavenworth. The revisions to the military program include the following: (1) Expanded use of airborne infantry and paratroopers. (2) Intensified cooperation between ground forces and airborne forces. (3) Replacing the triangular divisions used in World War II with divisions composed of three combat units. (4) Using rockets and missiles for long-range bombardment. (5) Expanding the use of atomic bombs in radio-controlled missiles. (6) Taking the Arctic Ocean as the first line of defense for the American continent, with the Pacific and Atlantic Oceans as flanking defenses. (7) Intensified cooperation between the Army, civilians, and scientists. (8) Close cooperation between intelligence units and the Army, civilians, and scientists. (9) Organizing a strong air force with long-range bombing capabilities, training aviation detachments and air reserves. (10) Establishing a chemical warfare branch. (11) Developing radio-controlled missiles.

US Troop Numbers Sharply Declining [Report from our newspaper] Broadcast from Washington, 16th: A year ago, the total number of US troops was 12.1 million; a little over a year after Japan's surrender, the number of US troops has been reduced to 2.3 million, about one-sixth of the wartime peak strength. By the end of June next year, the number of US troops will be reduced again to 1,615,200, but this number only represents the "core" of the US Army, Navy, and Air Force, which can be rapidly expanded, making it more powerful than before Pearl Harbor. At that time, the US military could muster 450,000 troops.

Nimitz Discusses Troop Reductions [United Press, Philadelphia, USA, 16th] Chief of Naval Operations Nimitz declared here today that the US Navy currently has 500,000 personnel, one-sixth of the peak number during the war, which is large enough. He advocated an annual review in order to gradually reduce the number. All US Navy personnel who wish to leave have been allowed to do so, except for 3,000 naval personnel who remain in hospitals to care for wounded soldiers. Just as one cannot consider soldiers to be useless roots. As of today, science has yet to invent something that can replace soldiers.

Hungarian Opposition Leader Advocates Forming a Fourth Power: An Alliance of Small European Nations with France to Participate in UN Activities 50

[Reuters, Budapest, 15th] The leader of Hungary's newly formed opposition Liberal Party, Szurdiuk, advocates that smaller European nations form an alliance with France to create a "fourth power." Szurdiuk stated in parliament that current world affairs are directed by the three major powers. Britain is too far or too close to the continent, the United States is in the Americas, and the Soviet Union itself is equivalent to a continent. Hungary should not become an appendage of any of the aforementioned three powers. France is the most culturally advanced power on the European continent. Although France is still busy dealing with its internal affairs, I believe that France will soon regain its position in major political events. Smaller European nations must rally around France to form a fourth power and participate in the work of the United Nations. Szurdiuk's speeches show that his Liberal Party is a left-wing democratic and Catholic party.

London Conference Resumes Yesterday: Britain Will Invite Arabs to Participate 52

Jewish Representatives May Attend

In a small guardhouse, as many as 57 men and women were detained, sitting with their knees bent for countless hours, and were not released for months.
