· Visiting Engineering Facilities in the Second District · Two Major Scenic Spots Restored to Their Former Glory · Longhua Pagoda and City God Temple Have a New Look · Two Hundred Stalls Will Rent Space at Small World to Operate 95

[Special Report from Our Newspaper] At 2:00 PM yesterday, the reporter followed Wu Wenhua, director of the Second District Engineering Management Office of the Municipal Public Works Bureau, Specialist Qian Weifan, Engineer Xu Dexian, and others to visit the engineering facilities in the Second District. In order to achieve division of labor, cooperation, and greater efficiency, the Public Works Bureau divided the engineering facilities into six districts. The so-called Second District includes most of the area east of the former French Concession's Zhengzhong South Road, the entire old walled city of Nanshi, along Xujiahui Road to Caohejing, Minhang, and other places, and also manages the entire Pudong area. We boarded a large truck from the Public Works Bureau and departed from the YMCA in Baxianqiao, to Longhua, then to Nanshi, visited the City God Temple, and then returned to our original route.

Remembering Jinji Road: Greatest Contribution

The characteristic of the Second District of the Public Works Bureau is that it possesses two historical scenic spots – Longhua Pagoda and the City God Temple. Both of these major sites were broken and incomplete during the eight years of war, with a desolate appearance! In the past year, with the full cooperation of the citizens and the authorities, most of them have been restored. The clay Bodhisattvas in the temples are painted brightly, and from the top of the Longhua Pagoda, you can overlook the iron birds rising and falling in the airport. These were all automatically raised funds by the local leaders to repair them. It is believed that more pious men and women will come to the temple next spring to burn incense. The greatest contribution of the Second District of the Public Works Bureau here is the widening of Jinji Road – the only avenue from the city center to Longhua – by one meter on each side. In the future, the crowded conditions on this road during the incense season will definitely be greatly improved.

Lotus Pond – Removing Silt

After visiting Longhua Pagoda, we turned to the City God Temple. The City God Temple is a commercial and recreational center, constantly handling a large number of tourists throughout the years. The destruction it suffered during the long war was even more severe, with many buildings collapsing and burning. The reconstruction of the City God Temple after the recovery was initiated by local people. After the Public Works Bureau agreed, a reorganization committee was organized, and all expenses were jointly funded by the citizens and the government. Now, it is all completed. The largest project was the removal of silt from the Lotus Pond of the City God Temple. People who have visited the City God Temple know that the Lotus Pond under the Nine-Bend Bridge has always been used by old Buddhist ladies as a release pond. It was originally a stagnant pool, and it is unknown how many years had passed. Tourists continuously threw garbage into the river, so it had long been foul-smelling.

Catching Turtles – Open Secret

The Public Works Bureau believed that this pool of sewage not only detracted from the view but also directly affected the health of countless people. Therefore, in May of this year, it thoroughly replaced this pool of ten thousand gallons of sewage! The fire brigade was responsible for the pumping project. It is said that when the water was drained, in addition to a small number of fish, there were countless turtles of all sizes left on the silt. The people who sold turtles inevitably took the opportunity to catch them. In fact, the people who caught the turtles must also be the people who sold the turtles. It is unknown what those who specialize in releasing animals to cultivate virtue think of this open secret?

Small World – Splendid

In addition, the Small World near the City God Temple was instantly turned into a rubble field by a wildfire during the war. Now, under the auspices of Huang Jinrong, Zong Cailiang, and others, a new Small World has been built, which is taller and more solid than the old one, and includes cinemas, cafes, open-air dance halls, storytelling houses, and other entertainment venues. According to Mr. Zong: The vacant second floor has been decided to be rented to vendors from the Zhubaoshan Road area, accommodating a total of two hundred stalls, all equipped with glass counters. The contract has now been signed, and the lessee, Datong Company, will receive a net income of 3 million yuan per month, which will be shared equally by the two hundred vendors. After the installation is completed, it will be open for business soon. Once the vendors are revived there, Small World will become the commercial and entertainment center of Nanshi, which is beyond doubt.

After this visit, the reporter deeply felt that Longhua Temple and the City God Temple, the two major scenic spots in the city, have indeed been restored. However, it is not enough to rely solely on the restoration of these two places. Moreover, what China needs after the revival is not just restoration, but creation!

Appendectomy Without Anesthesia · Forced to Stand at Attention for Ten Consecutive Days · Allied Prisoners of War Suffered Torture · Japanese War Criminal Kawashima Sentenced to Hanging · Matsuda Sentenced to Seven Years of Labor · 96

[Report from Our Newspaper] Kawashima, a medical officer at the Shenyang Forward Military Prisoner-of-War Camp, was sentenced to hanging by the U.S. Military Tribunal in this city for his confirmed atrocities against Allied prisoners of war. Matsuda, the director of the camp, was sentenced to seven years of labor for beating American prisoners of war and for failing to prevent the deaths of three American prisoners of war who were sentenced to death for attempting to escape during his tenure. Many Allied soldiers, heroes of the Battle of Bataan, were unfortunately captured due to the disparity in numbers and were detained in this concentration camp. When Prosecutor Major Fowler read out the depositions, he mentioned the testimony of General Wainwright, a hero of Bataan, who denied the rumors of any communication with Matsuda. Another witness was American medic Humberstone, who stated that according to Matsuda's orders, Japanese soldiers gave prisoners of war with severe pneumonia only three centimeters of thiamine powder per day, and even this small amount was withheld when the prisoners' temperature dropped slightly. American Sergeant Cole was suffering from appendicitis when he was arrested, and Kawashima deliberately delayed his treatment. Only when his appendix ruptured did he allow him to enter the hospital for surgery. In 1944, Kawashima refused to isolate patients with mumps from their companions, resulting in the infection of one-third of the prisoners of war. Sergeant Cole's testimony was particularly tragic. He wrote that he was sent to the hospital for surgery three days after suffering from appendicitis. At that time, the anesthetic had been used up, so he had to undergo the English surgery while fully conscious. Occasionally, when he groaned or cried out in pain, Kawashima would hit him on the head and shout, "No noise!" After the surgery was completed, Kawashima ordered him to get up from the operating table and walk to the bed himself. Kawashima had two nicknames in the concentration camp, one was "Butcher" and the other was "No Noise".

Sergeant Reynerson testified that one day, when the prisoners of war returned to the camp after labor, Kawashima ordered the sick to step forward. About eight or nine people responded, most of whom suffered from frostbite, with their toes frozen to a purplish-black color. Kawashima ordered them to take off their shoes and socks and stand on the ice. At that time, the weather was already twenty-one degrees below zero. Kawashima severely reprimanded them, saying that there was no such thing as "frostbite" in the world, and then allowed them to leave.

Another American sergeant, Lai, testified that he had witnessed Matsuda's assistant, Miki, beat four prisoners of war with a wooden stick three feet long and half an inch thick. He said that Miki severely beat these four people on the head below the ears, and they often fell to the ground after being hit. He continued to beat them until they could not move, and said that this was one way to educate the American army. He said that the American army was like beasts and should be treated like beasts. Miki claimed to be 30 years old and a graduate of the Economics Department of Tokyo Imperial University. He admitted to insulting about ten to fifteen American soldiers. He has now been sentenced to twenty years of hard labor.

Miki mentioned the execution of the three American prisoners who attempted to escape: The execution was carried out on July 13, 1943. They were first blindfolded, then their arms were stretched out on a wooden cross, and they were ordered to sit down with their legs crossed. From seven or eight meters away, the Japanese gunmen knelt down and aimed at them, one shooting the head and one shooting the chest, firing one shot at a time for fun.

Another American lieutenant proved that he had witnessed a Japanese officer grinding the face of an American sailor with the heel of his leather shoe. Another American prisoner of war was ordered to stand at attention for ten consecutive days, during which he was only allowed to sleep for ten hours.

It is noted that American lawyer Courtenay and several Japanese lawyers were retained on behalf of the defendant at this trial.

Ministry of Education Issues Nationwide Order Promoting National Education and Limiting Fees 101

[Our Nanjing News] In order to popularize national education, after the Ministry of Education promulgated the Second Five-Year Implementation Plan this year, it is urgently necessary to conduct a thorough investigation of whether various provinces and cities have increased the number of central national schools and Bao national schools in accordance with the plan and to seek promotion. The Ministry of Education is promoting the popularization of national education on the one hand, and taking care of poor students on the other hand. Moreover, national education is compulsory education and should not be charged. Therefore, a special order is issued nationwide to limit fees, so that families in difficult circumstances can easily enroll. All of these must be observed from the field and promoted and improved. Tang Deyuan, a member of the National Education Guidance Committee, has been sent to inspect the current status of the implementation of national education in the recovery of education in the provinces and cities of North China. Tang has already set off on an inspection tour. The extent to which national education has progressed in the cities of Beijing and Shanghai and other provinces and cities will also be followed up with the dispatch of personnel for inspection. Furthermore, since the provinces and cities have greatly increased the number of Bao national schools in accordance with the Five-Year Implementation Plan for National Education, a large number of teachers are needed. The Ministry of Education has taken this into account in the Educational Administrative Plan for the thirty-sixth year, and has given flexibility to provinces and cities that cultivate teachers for the promotion of national education. For example, in cases where teachers are urgently needed, short-term teacher training can be carried out according to the actual situation, and even a one-year simple teacher training program is not impossible. For the current emergency, the method of using substitute teachers can be adopted, and the standards can be raised and training increased at an appropriate time. Because national education originally had a stage of four years of primary school and two years of senior primary school, simple teachers can teach those with four years of education in Bao schools, it is said.

Hao Gengsheng's Report on Inspection of the Northeast: Students' Meals Lack Oil, Only Boiled Salted Soybeans as Accompaniment; Teachers Have Not Received Salaries, Voluntarily Teaching for Four Months 106

[Our Nanjing News] Hao Gengsheng, an inspector appointed by the Ministry of Education, submitted a report to the Ministry of Education on the inspection of education in the Northeast. A brief account was published in this newspaper yesterday. His inspection reports on Northeast China University, Changchun University, and Jilin University have also been submitted to the Ministry. A more detailed account is now published below:

Sale of Enemy and Puppet Property Reaches 500 Million

(1) Preparatory Office of the Private Northeast China University: The school will set up five colleges of Liberal Arts, Law, Science, Engineering, and Agriculture. The Colleges of Liberal Arts and Law will use the former Xingya Hall, which has spacious buildings. The Colleges of Science and Engineering will use the old site of the former Fengtian Industrial University in Tiexi (the Japanese spent 1.5 million yen to build the school), with buildings covering an area of more than 13,000 square meters. Among them, the main equipment has been transported away, and there is still a part of the remaining equipment that can be used. The College of Agriculture is located on Siping Street, which was originally a Japanese farm with a large scale. Regarding the funds, the proceeds from the sale of enemy and puppet property reached 500 million [currency unit unclear] in currency. The school's application for record filing is being actively processed. An official document has already been submitted to the ministry. At the same time, Du Yuming, the chairman of the school's board of directors, has sent a special letter to the minister explaining everything.

Palace-Style Construction with Heating Equipment

(2) Changchun University, which is about to be established: The school plans to set up five colleges of Liberal Arts, Law, Science, Engineering, and Agriculture. The College of Agriculture was originally the site of the Jian Country University of the puppet Manchukuo. The Jian Country University was directly under the puppet Manchukuo State Council, and the students were mostly civil servants undergoing training. The buildings are mostly palace-style, and the auditorium can accommodate at least 3,000 people. The floor is damaged, the seats are empty, and the heating equipment is still intact. Not far from the school is a Jian Country Martyrs' Shrine, which is entirely palace-style and beautifully constructed. Although some of the buildings have bullet marks, the building itself is generally undamaged. The scale of this temple is grand and can be used by Changchun University, but it is still under consideration and has not yet been determined. The Colleges of Liberal Arts and Law are located in the former puppet Ministry of Education. The equipment is incomplete, and the buildings are not greatly damaged. They can be used after repairing the doors and windows. The College of Engineering will use the former Xinjing Industrial University, which has not been much damaged and is currently occupied by the military. The College of Medicine was originally the Xinjing Medical University, with all of its equipment intact. The spirit of the students and nurses is excellent. In the past, almost all of the professors were Japanese. Currently, Guo Songgen from Taiwan is working hard to maintain the school. He has been temporarily appointed as acting president by Special Envoy Zang to maintain the school's affairs. Adjustments will be made after the preparatory personnel of Changchun University arrive. There are currently 186 students. The class situation at the college is very good. To prevent cholera, students have given lectures and administered injections on the streets, and their service spirit is excellent. Among the students in Changchun who plan to enter Changchun University, 800 to 900 are from Shenyang, and nearly 1,000 are from Harbin and other places. The students and school buildings of the school do not seem to be a problem. The key is to have someone in charge to prepare for the opening of school as soon as possible. Gengsheng urged Director Huang in Beiping to go there on a fixed date, and it is said that he set off for Changchun on August 10th.

Sturdy Glass Windows Burned into Wavy Shapes

(3) Chinese Academy of Sciences: During the puppet Manchukuo period, the academy was the center for the Japanese to develop the rich resources of the Northeast and promote the expansion of its industrial national defense technology research. Although the scale of the scientific research institution is not very large, it includes many departments. After August 15th, some of the equipment was looted unsuccessfully and destroyed by burning. Although the library had fire prevention equipment, gasoline flames turned the books on the bookshelves to ashes, and the sturdy glass windows were burned into wavy shapes, which shows the intensity of the burning. The academy is now taken over by the Ministry of Economic Affairs. According to the academic research system, it seems that the Central Research Institute should continue to run it.

Local People Disappointed that Jilin University Will Not Be Restored

(4) Jilin University Tutorial Classes are located at the old site of the former Jilin University. Jilin University was completed before September 18th. Its predecessor was the Higher Normal School in the 25th year of the Republic of China. In the 27th year, the Japanese changed it to the Shidao Higher School, and in the 31st year, it was changed to the Shidao University. At that time, there were more than 1,700 students. After August 15th, troops were stationed there, and students and faculty members spontaneously organized to protect the school, so the damage to the school property was limited, and the loss was minimal (troops had been stationed there seven times in the past). There are currently 25 faculty members (14 staff members) and 353 students, including 59 female students. There are 25 faculty residences, which can accommodate 40 families. There are more than 30,000 books. The chemical instruments were damaged, but fortunately the total loss is less than 25%. Currently, remedial classes are being offered. The funds are raised by the faculty and students of the school from all parties. After Gengsheng and Special Envoy Zang inspected the school, the Special Envoy's Office agreed to allocate a subsidy of 450,000 [currency unit unclear] per month. The students of the school live a hard life, and their meals lack oil, so they only cook salted soybeans as a side dish. Since August 15th, the teachers have not received their salaries and have been voluntarily teaching for nearly four months. The school buildings are suitable for use as a normal school. Local people in Jilin are very enthusiastic about restoring the original Jilin University. Chairman Liang once gathered local people and explained to Gengsheng the reasons for restoring Jilin University as follows: (1) The provincial government has long paid attention to this matter and resolved at the provincial government committee meeting to restore Jilin University as soon as possible. (2) Restoring Jilin University is restoring an old school, not establishing a new one. (3) Changchun University is located too far west, not as suitable as Yongji. (4) Yongji has beautiful mountains and rivers and a higher cultural level, so it is hoped that there will be a university. (5) If limited to the regulations of the government school name, using the place name instead of the province name, then Yongji is the location of Jilin City and can still be called Jilin University. (6) Zhang Zuoxiang once used his own strength to run a university, but today the central government is not restoring it, which really disappoints the local people. When Gengsheng left Shenyang and Beiping, Chairman Han of Heilongjiang Province, Chairman Wu of Hejiang Province, and the heads of the education and finance departments of the two provinces also repeatedly requested to forward the request to restore Jilin University in a timely manner.

30,000 Artifacts Looted One After Another

(5) Museum: Originally Tang Yulin's residence, it was converted into a museum by the Japanese after September 18th. Currently, the Special Envoy's Office of the headquarters is also located here. However, most of the upper floor is occupied by the military's Special Envoy's Office and has not yet been read out. There are five ancient relic storage rooms inside. There were originally 37,803 ancient relics, which were looted one after another. For example, the Buddha statues in the Rehe Imperial Palace that could not be taken away were destroyed. What remains are only inscriptions and stone carvings. The Northeast Cultural Relics Preservation Committee is now preparing to be established to sort out the lost relics. It is planned to appoint Mr. Jin Yuzhan as the director to be responsible for the work.

Former Stable Wen Su Ge Has Many Ming Dynasty Archives

(6) (Thirteen) Library: The library is located in the old palace, formerly known as Wen Su Ge. It stores the Complete Library of the Four Branches of Literature, including 9,071 volumes of the Zibu, 12,265 volumes of the Jibu, 9,408 volumes of the History Department, 5,509 volumes of the Classics Department, and 5,020 volumes of the Palace Edition of the Illustrated Compendium of Books. In addition, there are 127 volumes of the Palace Edition of the General Catalogue of the Complete Library of the Four Branches of Literature and 72 volumes of the Textual Research of the Complete Library of the Four Branches of Literature. In addition to the 41,273 volumes of the Complete Library of the Four Branches of Literature, there are 150,000 other books. The library contains many archives from the Ming Dynasty, and there is also an extremely valuable book by the Japanese Shimayo, which is also stored in the library. Shimayo originally wanted to sell it, and we are willing to keep it for use. This issue has not yet been resolved. The Wen Su Ge library has solid construction and is fireproof. The bookshelves are all made of steel, and the doors and windows are covered with iron sheets to ensure safety.

Feng Yong University Temporarily Not Planning to Restore

(7) In addition, according to President Feng himself, Shenyang Private Feng Yong University is not planning to restore this year because the school's property cannot be recovered and the source of funds has been cut off. Due to factual difficulties, I was unable to visit the above-mentioned schools in Harbin, but the general situation can be known from the process of Mayor Yang's filing of the Harbin Maintaining Education Ministry's Directly-Managed University. All adjustments to the schools above the junior college level in the Northeast region, except for the schools in the unrecovered areas, are generally in line with the methods indicated by the Ministry.

Public Office Candidate Review Certificate to Have Stamp Affixed by the Holder 117

The Examination Yuan's Old Election Committee yesterday sent a letter to the municipal government regarding the postage fees for public office candidate review certificates. It has been stipulated that (1) The stamp will be purchased and affixed by the certificate holder in accordance with the number stipulated in the Stamp Tax Law, and a private seal will be affixed to the stamp. This committee will no longer collect it on their behalf. (2) The cost of the certificate will be uniformly changed to 30 [currency unit unclear] for both types A and B, except for provinces without examination and evaluation offices, where the cost of type B certificates will still be determined by the province and reported to the Yuan for record (type B will be changed after the provincial government's handling of the review and transfer business is transferred to the examination and evaluation office for reception). (3) The postage fee will be changed to the standard collection rate set by the Postal Administration for each registered mail item (currently 50 [currency unit unclear]).

Public Administration Personnel Intensive Training - The First Training Session Concludes 118

The Municipal Government's Department of Civil Affairs conducted an intensive training program for public administration personnel in the city. The first training session, which began on the 11th of this month, featured an exceptionally tight schedule, keeping the department's staff extremely busy. On the afternoon of the 13th, a practice exercise was held to re-verify household registrations. All 280-plus trainees were divided into 57 groups, led by instructors to the 81st Bao in the Fifth District for on-site re-verification. On the morning of the 14th, the results of the re-verification were transcribed. Each trainee also presented the difficulties encountered during the household registration re-verification and transcription for discussion in small group meetings in the afternoon. Instructors answered each question one by one. Finally, at 5:00 PM, Section Chief Chen delivered a closing speech before the trainees were dismissed. The trainees expressed great interest in this training and gained considerable knowledge and experience in public administration. They felt that the training period was too short and that they should maintain contact with each other in their future work to jointly seek improvements. To foster camaraderie among the graduating trainees, they suggested to Section Chief Chen that a alumni association be organized and a directory published. Section Chief Chen immediately agreed to plan this after the training of all public administration personnel in the city is completed. It is reported that the second and third training sessions will begin simultaneously on the 18th.

Instructions for Completing the Household Re-Verification Form

The Second Section of the Shanghai Municipal Government's Department of Civil Affairs has recently compiled "Instructions for Completing the Household Re-Verification Form Before Registration Transcription," as follows:

Re-verifying household registrations before transcribing them into the registry is of utmost importance. Because this is the first time setting up a household registry, the obligor is not required to fill out another household registration application. The household survey form will serve as the application. Since the household survey was conducted in this city in February, there have been many discrepancies between the household information recorded on the household survey form and the actual household situation. Therefore, the original household survey form cannot be rashly used as the basis for transcription. A household re-verification must be carried out before transcription.

Secondly, existing household survey forms contain many errors because (1) the personnel handling the initial household survey were unfamiliar with the form-filling methods, and (2) the laws and regulations have changed repeatedly, leaving the form-fillers at a loss. If transcription is based on these errors, the errors will be compounded. Correcting errors after household registration is cumbersome, so a detailed re-verification must be carried out before transcription to avoid registration errors.

Now that the transcription work is about to begin, we must clearly recognize the following points before re-verifying household registrations: (1) There must be absolutely no errors in any of the household registration fields. Therefore, the household survey form must be accurately recorded before transcription. (2) After household registration begins, household administration in this city will be brought onto the right track, and there should no longer be any inaccurate household registration information. (3) To ensure the accuracy of household registration, it must start with the household. Every household and every individual must be accurately recorded. One Jia, one Bao, and even the entire city will be accurate. Therefore, every citizen and every re-verification staff member must recognize this point, cherish household administration in this city, and not be careless or sloppy with household re-verification.

To ensure accurate re-verification, the form-filling methods for each field of the household survey form are explained in detail below for reference by the citizens of this city and all levels of public administration personnel. Furthermore, these instructions are a unified regulation for past form-filling methods. In the future, all application forms and registration books shall be filled out in accordance with these instructions.

1. Relationship to Head of Household The "Relationship to Head of Household" explains the identity relationship of each member within the household. The identity relationship of each member within a common household is centered on the head of household. Therefore, how each member is related is based on the head of household as the referent. When surveying a household, it is easy to make mistakes if someone other than the head of household answers the surveyor. For example, if the head of household is the "father," and the "second son" answers during the survey, the "eldest daughter-in-law" may mistakenly answer as "sister-in-law." Therefore, when citizens answer surveyors or fill out application forms themselves, they should use the tone of the head of household so that the relationship of each person is not mistaken. Survey personnel should pay more attention to this type of error during surveys. The identity relationship of each member within a common business household can be filled out according to each person's position within the business organization, such as "accountant" or "shopkeeper" in a store, or "teacher" or "student" in a school.

2. Name "Name" is a person's identifying mark in society. A person's rights and obligations are based on their name. Therefore, the name entered should be the name commonly used in society. Pseudonyms, assumed names, or a woman's customary use of "So-and-so Shi" should not be used. The "Regulations on Restrictions on the Use of Names" promulgated by the National Government on July 17, 1941, contain the following provisions regarding names, which demonstrate that filling out the name when registering a household must be done with caution.

(Article 1) A citizen of the Republic of China shall have only one given name. The name registered in the household registry is the given name. A person using a courtesy name or pseudonym shall indicate their given name. (Article 2) The acquisition, establishment, transfer, or alteration of property rights shall be done using the given name or by indicating the given name. (Article 3) If shared property is used under a trade name or other name, the given names of the co-owners shall be indicated. If the total number of co-owners exceeds twenty, only the given names of the representatives may be indicated. (Article 6) In response to a lawful investigation by a public official, the given name shall be reported. Failure to use the given name shall be punishable by detention or a fine of one hundred yuan or less.

3. Gender Indicate male or female. (To be continued)

Stock Exchange's First Day of Trading Sees Over 4 Million Shares Traded - Bull Market Shows High Prices but Lackluster Momentum - Collective Accounting at 5 PM Yields Good Results 119

[Our Report] The Stock Exchange officially opened trading on various listed stocks at 10:00 AM yesterday. After a bull market opening, trading was generally stable. The atmosphere was also quite relaxed. After two hours of trading, prices of all stocks trended downwards.

At 9:50 AM, Chairman of the Board Du Yong, General Manager Wang Zhixin, Assistant Managers Yang Yinbo and Gu Shanchang, Chief Secretary Hua Wenyu, Manager Chen Xubi, and Deputy Manager Zhang Jisan entered the trading floor in succession. At exactly 10:00 AM, Du himself rang the opening bell. As the bell rang, each trading counter began its bull market. Five minutes later, the bull markets for each stock opened. The bell rang again, and official trading began. The shouts of brokers buying and selling immediately followed.

Yesterday's market in general was relatively stable. Due to psychological factors, blue-chip stocks ("two big, three small") and a few unpopular mid-sized stocks saw high prices in the bull market opening. After opening prices were established, bullish investors took profits, gradually being pressured by sellers. However, financial backers intermittently provided some support, so although the process was lackluster, there were many fluctuations. Throughout the market, only the unpopular small stocks Huafeng Enamel and Liann Department Store stood out. The former was boosted by scattered speculative funds, and the latter deliberately pushed up its price near noon, ending at a high price. However, trading in these two stocks was not widespread. As a result, compared to the previous closing, Yong'an Textile and Meiya (probably a stock abbreviation) fell slightly, while Jingfu, Xinguang, and Qinxing each fell half a percent. Among unpopular stocks, besides Huafeng and Lian'an being the most prominent, the former rose slightly, while the latter opened low but rose by over 20%, ending at the highest price, resulting in a sharp increase of 40% compared to last Saturday. The rest fell slightly. Mid-sized stocks saw a rebound of half a percent.

Yesterday's price limits for each stock were calculated separately based on the bull market opening prices of each stock. In the future, the price limits for each stock will be calculated separately based on the previous day's closing price.

Yesterday, the total number of shares traded was 4,347,400. The stock with the highest trading volume was Yong'an Textile Factory, reaching 1.2 million shares. Jingfu also had nearly 500,000 shares. The trading volume of Xinguang, Qinxing, and Yong'an Company stocks also exceeded 300,000 shares each. China Textile and China Silk Industry had lower volumes, both under 10,000 shares.

At 5:00 PM, all brokers gathered at the market to collectively close their accounts. By 6:39 PM, all accounts were balanced. The Stock Exchange authorities were satisfied. The Stock Exchange also posted several announcements in the stock market yesterday. The important ones are summarized below:

Announcement No. 14: When delivering shares, each broker must attach the following documents to each share certificate: 1. A securities delivery voucher must be attached to the front of the share certificate. 2. The following must be attached to the back of the share certificate:

(1) Share transfer application form. (2) Share trading record form. (3) Share sale contract (red or blue is acceptable). All of the above must be stamped with the broker's official seal.

Announcement No. 15: Regarding securities settlement matters, please pay attention to the following points, listed separately: 1. For the convenience of settlement, each broker should submit bank drafts that can be exchanged, and must stamp the back of the draft with the broker's name and number seal. 2. To ensure smooth settlement for each broker, it is more convenient for even-numbered firms to open accounts with the Bank of China, and odd-numbered firms to open accounts with the Trust Department of the Bank of Communications. 3. Due to exchange time constraints, collections are from 9:00 AM to 11:00 AM. 4. Securities received are limited to 11:30 AM to 2:00 PM. 5. Securities issued are limited to 9:30 AM to 11:30 AM the next morning. 6. Payment for goods issued is limited to 1:00 PM to 3:00 PM.

Central Bank Posts Daily Exchange Rates for Inward and Outward Trade 128

[Central News Agency, Shenyang, 16th] Regarding the issue of industrial and commercial remittances, the Economic Committee of the Northeast Headquarters decided to handle it in accordance with the "Implementation Measures for Industrial and Commercial Remittances in the Nine Northeastern Provinces" promulgated in mid-September. The exchange rate between the nine northeastern provinces and the interior will be determined by the Central Bank posting daily rates. The exchange rate from the Northeast to Tianjin and Beiping is 1 to 11.5 yuan. The exchange rate from Tianjin and Beiping to the Northeast is 1 to 22.5 yuan. Except for remittances from military and government agencies, which are remitted by the Central Bank at the posted exchange rate, ordinary remittances are temporarily handled by the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the Farmers Bank, and the Central Trust Bureau. In the past, public servants' family support remittances handled by the Central Bank will also be handled as ordinary remittances from now on. The difference between the old and new exchange rates will be subsidized by the Headquarters to prevent public servants from suffering losses due to exchange rate fluctuations. Furthermore, the ordinary exchange rate originally changes at any time depending on various factors such as market capital supply and demand, trade exports, and price levels. However, in order to stabilize the financial situation, the Central Bank will strive to keep the exchange rate stable and avoid many changes.

Double Horse Price Unchanged - 2,300 Bales of Yarn Distributed - Yarn Firms Get a Share - Market Is Flat and Lackluster - Piece Goods Sales Are Not Strong - Foundation Is Still Solid 130

[Our Report] The Silk Factory Joint Distribution Committee convened a regular meeting at 3:00 PM yesterday, selling a standard quota of 20-count cotton yarn. Private factories were fully allocated according to their application amounts. In addition to the factories directly producing the textiles, Fangjian will also allocate to yarn firms according to their applications.

The yarn market was calm and uneventful yesterday. Because the Minyue gang had no ships and the route was blocked, large Double Horse yarn saw few inquiries. The market had a dismal outlook. Small and medium-sized yarns were purchased by the Changjiang gang. The supply and demand was balanced and the market was unchanged. The market gradually declined near noon. The initial price of 42-count Blue Phoenix was 2.3 million yuan, which later became 2.24 million yuan. The initial price of old Double Horse yarn was 1.5 million yuan, which later fell by 50,000 yuan. The new Singles initially fell from around 1.4 million to 1.35 million yuan.

The slump in business in the Southern gang is partly due to the lack of control over visa exports. Therefore, they all detour to Jiangxi for transport, which, although time-consuming, is still profitable. However, the inability to transport grain along that line smoothly has affected their revenue.

The cloth market remains old. Blue V-shaped cloth is 62,000 yuan. 3A Rainbow Ball is 62,500 yuan. Unbranded Rainbow Ball is priced at 55,500 yuan. The Dragon Head has not opened. Although the price is 27,500 yuan, there are no goods. Four Gentlemen Serge is priced as high as 65,500 yuan, because Fangjian has not distributed it several times. In short, yesterday the entire market was flat. Sales have not been brisk. Inventory is also lacking. The foundation is still solid.

Hong Kong's Ban on Cloth Exports Can Stabilize Yarn Prices - Official of Fangjian Says 131

An official in charge of the business division of China Textile Construction Company recently expressed the following opinions on the Hong Kong authorities' formal order to ban the export of cotton cloth from the 15th of this month: (1) Hong Kong's adoption of this strict measure was implemented at the request of Premier Song Ziwen. (2) Smuggling in South China is extremely rampant, and the smuggling and tax evasion will be eliminated immediately. (3) Smuggled cotton yarn in South China is woven into cloth in Hong Kong and then transported to the South Sea Islands. However, the current exchange rate in the South Sea has not been determined, so it cannot be allowed to leak out at will. The official finally stated that Hong Kong's ban on cotton cloth exports would be sufficient to maintain stable yarn prices.

United States Faces Difficulties in Reducing Tariff Barriers - Many Countries Still Advocate Protectionist Policies 133

[United Press, Washington, 15th] The high tariff policies adopted by countries such as India, Brazil, Mexico, Chile, and Australia have made the US plan to reduce pre-war trade barriers more complicated. Autumn Cocoon Loan of 15 Billion Officially Released Today - Farmers Bank and Borrowing Cocoon Merchants to Sign Loan Contracts Today 134

The autumn cocoon loan for this year was originally scheduled to begin lending yesterday. However, due to incomplete procedures, it has been changed to officially lend out today. Over 40 companies have applied for loans in recent days. Farmers Bank will sign contracts with the borrowing cocoon merchants today. China Silk Company will also continue to handle unfinished procedures with Farmers Bank this morning. The company will also meet with Farmers Bank and cocoon factory company officials this afternoon to jointly review the qualifications of borrowers. It is reported that the total amount of the loan is temporarily set at 15 billion, which can reel about 5,000 piculs of raw silk. Among them, 4,200 piculs of funds will be loaned to manufacturers who obtained loans in the spring cocoon loan. The remaining 800 piculs of funds will be loaned to newly opened silk factories. The principle is 3.5 piculs for old-style silk reeling machines and 4.5 piculs for new-style silk reeling machines. As for manufacturers who violated the spring cocoon loan and manufacturers who did not start reeling silk after purchasing spring cocoons, their autumn cocoon loan rights will be revoked.

Record of the Recovery of Chengde 144

— Central News Agency dispatch from Chaoyang, 9th

Rehe fell to the enemy in the year following the September 18th Incident, held captive for thirteen years. The people longed day and night for the motherland to liberate them. When the Japanese devils surrendered with a thunderclap, men, women, old and young were overjoyed. Last year, during the Mid-Autumn Festival, unfamiliar Eighth Route Army troops arrived. They were mistaken for National Revolutionary Army, and welcomed with joy. After a period of time, they received the "blessings" of this fake National Revolutionary Army, which only brought struggle, and extortionate levies, and the people became lost. During this time of unclear authenticity, the Communist army invaded and occupied Chengde, Chifeng, and various counties in northern Rehe. The National Revolutionary Army recovering the northern frontier was blocked east of Pingquan, and south of Gushan (70 li south of Chifeng). In May, they were forced to retreat from Gushan to Yebaishou, and from then on, the northwest of Rehe was plunged into deep water and scorching fire.

Counterattack Begins, Rapid Advance　Thereafter, the people of Chifeng and Chengde counties, unable to bear the harassment of the Communist army, repeatedly sent representatives to meet with General Shi Jue, the military commander of the National Revolutionary Army, and Liu Duoquan, chairman of the provincial government, requesting a speedy advance to relieve them from their plight. The authorities were always constrained by the ceasefire agreement, and unable to advance. This not only went against the wishes of the people, but also caused misunderstandings among middle and lower-ranking officers and soldiers. Especially after the retreat from Gushan, the officers and soldiers of the 13th Army suffered illegal attacks from the Communist army day and night, and were almost consumed by anger. This time, in order to thwart the Communist army's conspiracy to attack the National Revolutionary Army and open up eastern Hebei, the 13th Army issued an order to advance to meet the enemy. The soldiers rubbed their fists and showed smiles, no longer complaining about their superiors.

The counterattack began on August 27th. The 13th Army was responsible for the northern route, heading straight for Chifeng from Yebaishou. The plan was to recover the territory by September 5th, but the mission was completed on August 29th. The 100 kilometers of rugged mountain roads took only two and a half days. On the same day, the northern route also recovered Gubei, and the next day crossed the Heishui River, reaching Nailin, within the borders of Chifeng. The speed of the advance was sufficient to prove the strength of the National Revolutionary Army. At the same time, Chairman Liu Dongkui personally braved danger, leading the civilian workers to repair the roads along with the army. The residents nearby braved the hail of bullets to carry water to the front lines, entirely out of their own volition. This showed the spirit of cooperation between the military, government, officials and people everywhere, and their hatred for the Communist army.

Beautiful Outline Completely Deformed

In mid-June, this reporter wrote an article titled "Chengde Weekly," introducing the beautiful outline of Chengde. Now, this beautiful city is deformed. The Communist army destroyed and plundered while retreating, leaving the city without electricity, the houses damaged, and the wealth gone. The airport, the smallest in scale and the only one with an asphalt runway in all of Rehe, was also damaged beyond repair. Everywhere exposed traces of the Communist army's thieving acts. However, when asked, the merchants and civilians who had been swept clean said, "Although our belongings are gone, spiritually, it's like a shackle has been lifted." Yes, they feel relieved to have received the army of the motherland.

Although most of the shops in the market have reopened, business is still sluggish for the following reasons: (1) Nineteen out of ten old shops were struggled against and liquidated. For months, the prosperous Nanyingzi Street trade was monopolized by the Communist Party's agency cooperatives. Before the retreat, official and private goods were swept away and plundered westward. (2) The Communist army used the "Legal Tender" extensively, issuing border currency in excess. During the retreat, they plundered the Legal Tender that civilians had saved, and fled with it fully loaded. After the recovery, no one accepted the border currency, and Legal Tender and circulating notes were difficult to use as chips. (3) The Pingquan-Gubei and Jinzhou-Gubei roads are not open, and daily necessities are not easily transported from Beiping or Jinzhou in the short term. This year, Rehe is expected to have a good harvest, and food is not a problem in itself, but Chengde is currently experiencing a shortage. White rice and flour are nowhere to be seen. This is all a temporary phenomenon. After Shi Jue took office as the Chengde Garrison Commander, he calmed the military and civilians while rushing to repair the destroyed buildings. The order of the market is recovering extremely quickly.

Rushing to Repair Day and Night to Provide Support

The highway and railway from Pingquan to Chengde were thoroughly destroyed. The roadbed could not be seen, and not a single sleeper was left. A few steel rails could be seen intermittently, lying crookedly on the distant slopes. Not a single iron bridge was intact. In addition to slogans slandering the head of state, the bridge piers also had white slogans such as "Build a Democratic Country" and "Build a New Rehe." This "build" slogan was painted on the destroyed bridge piers, which could be called a great farce. Wan Guobin, director of the Jinzhou Railway Bureau, and Li Xian, brigadier general and commander of the engineer corps of the Northeast Security Command, have followed the army westward, supervising the staff to rush to repair day and night. The Lingyuan-Pingquan section is expected to be completed within days. If it can be repaired to Chengde, then once the Jinzhou-Chengde Railway is open, Chengde can undoubtedly be declared prosperous. Chairman Liu Duoquan followed the army west on August 27th. After Chengde was captured, he returned to Chaoyang once, instructing the various departments and offices of the provincial government to prepare to return to Chengde. Without even warming his seat, he and Commissioner Li Shoulien led the Chengde, Luanping, and other county magistrates westward in haste. He arrived in Pingquan yesterday, and is heading to Chengde today. Various departments of the provincial government have also transferred a number of personnel to Chengde to take over the relevant business. A provincial government office has been established in Chengde, and it is expected that all personnel can be fully repatriated within a month. According to Chairman Liu's words to the reporter, all preparations are in place, waiting only for the availability of transportation. Chief Education Officer Liu said that "after the schools in Chengde are restored, the greatest difficulty is finding teachers, especially for middle schools." It is said that Chairman Liu is also determined to do his best to improve this. The reporter hereby sends a message to scholars in Beiping and Tianjin to consider this.

Reader's Opinions 145

— Regulations

(1) This column is absolutely open, and the illiterate are responsible for their own reading. But avoid being verbose. (2) Do not attack private individuals, and do not submit the same manuscript to multiple publications. (3) Contributors must write "Reader's Opinion Manuscript" and provide their real name and address, but may use a pen name when published. (4) This column does not pay for manuscripts. (5) This newspaper has the right to edit submissions. (6) Whether or not a submission is published will not be notified. (7) This newspaper may, when necessary, forward submissions to relevant agencies for reference.

Opinions on Selling Sugar at Controlled Prices

This city is selling sugar at controlled prices again, which is truly a blessing for the citizens. Although there have been several sales before, the order was very chaotic. In the end, it was still the young and strong who benefited. Moreover, although the authorities stipulated that each person was limited to three catties, in reality, southern goods merchants used the excuse of general sales and limited each person to one or two catties. There were very few who sold according to the regulations of the authorities. This time, it is stipulated that each person is limited to two catties with their ID card, and the time is extended, with sales also in the morning, so the order is gradually improving. However, using ID cards is still not fair, because ID cards are only issued to people over the age of thirteen, so children under the age of thirteen do not have the fortune to enjoy it. In fact, children need more sugar than adults, especially babies. Therefore, I hope that next time, sales can be further improved, with each household using a household registration card to receive the sugar at once. This would greatly simplify the time and procedures. I hope the relevant authorities will pay attention. (Zhou Li)

Arbitrary Price Increases for Highway Bus Tickets

Editor: There are buses that go directly from Jianbi to Zhenjiang, departing every day in the morning and afternoon. A few days ago, they departed on time, with each ticket costing 800 yuan, and each bus carrying 30 people, selling tickets for 24,000 yuan. Yesterday afternoon, the bus from Zhenjiang to Jianbi, charged 2,000 yuan per person, with 22 passengers, totaling 44,000 yuan. They also did not sell tickets. I went to ask them why they did not sell tickets according to regulations? The staff replied in a nasty voice, "Those who want to ride can ride, what regulations?" I believe Zhenjiang is the capital of Jiangsu Province. Isn't the establishment of the highway for the convenience of the people? (Zhu Youming)

Please Restore Routes 1 and 9 Buses

Editor: I am a resident near Zhaofeng Park. In the past, there were Routes 1 and 9 buses from Zhaofeng Park that could go directly to the Bund, and there were also trolleybuses that could reach Jing'an Temple, which was very convenient for residents. Since the January 28th Incident, the buses have stopped running, relying only on trolleybuses, and the congestion is indescribable. Now that the War of Resistance has been won, public cars have been temporarily replaced in the public bureaus in various places, but only this place is still lacking. Why is the authorities favoring one over the other? The Zhaofeng Park area is a residential area, and residents travel back and forth to the central district several times a day. Moreover, there are passengers from the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway West Station, students from St. John's and Great China Universities, and visitors to Zhaofeng Park. The number of passengers is unparalleled. When Routes 1 and 9 buses were running in the past, it was also very crowded. Now, only three or four trolleybuses run between them. How can they be enough? As a result, visitors to Zhaofeng Park are becoming increasingly deserted. The misery of squeezing onto the bus is like escaping from a disaster. Now, temporary public cars are run every Sunday when the park holds concerts. It seems that the establishment of this car is only for the convenience of listening to music! If the cars could run according to the old Route 1, then the passengers at the trolleybus stops at Jing'an Temple, Seymour Road, Carter Road, and Chengdu Road would definitely not be so crowded. I hope the authorities will think twice. (Xu Bing)

Many Door Numbers Are Confused and Unclear

Editor: The door numbers of the shops and households along the lanes north of Zhongzheng Road are all made of tinplate, painted with white background and black characters. After years of disrepair, they have become unrecognizable. In many places, each household has two door numbers with different numbers. There are even those who deliberately remove the door numbers. I don't know what the purpose is. The door number is one of the addresses, which should not be ignored. I hope the relevant authorities will start to improve this immediately. (Zhang Qiu)

Unclean Lanes Hinder Hygiene

Editor: I am a student and live in Xicheng Lane, Ximen Road, Madang Road. The lane was originally very clean, but recently the entrance and bottom of the lane are extremely dirty. The reason is this: The street sweepers in the lane, citing that their salaries cannot be maintained, have gathered their fellow villagers and relatives to set up steamed bun stalls, etc., at the entrance of the lane, causing oil and water to splash everywhere and obstructing traffic. There was originally a wooden house at the bottom of the lane for the street sweepers to live in. Recently, they claimed that it was not easy to find a house, so their accomplices have been using the area next to the wooden house as a place to live, and storing a large amount of straw, raising chickens and ducks, and unlicensed fierce dogs (events of biting young children often occur). As a result, the stench is overwhelming, and cooking is done there, which is very easy to cause a fire. I hope the relevant authorities will take action to maintain local hygiene. (Cai Zhiping)
